## 广(廣)州( )
---
## Guangzhou
### Guǎngzhōu
---
- **traditional:** 廣州
- **definition:** Guangzhou
- **pinyin:** Guǎngzhōu
- **components:**
  - 广(廣)
    - guǎng
    - broad
  - 州
    - zhōu
    - state; region
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 廣 (guǎng, "broad") refers to the vastness or expansiveness, while 州 (zhōu, "state; region") is a term used historically for an administrative division or region.
  - **interpretation:** 廣州 (Guǎngzhōu, "Guangzhou") is named for its historical significance as a broad and expansive region within China. It reflects its status as a major and influential administrative area.
- **examples:**
  - 我打算明年去广(廣)州，体验当(體驗當)地文化。
    - Wǒ dǎsuàn míngnián qù Guǎngzhōu, tǐyàn dāngdì wénhuà.
    - I plan to go to Guangzhou next year to experience the local culture.
  - 广(廣)州是中国(國)的南方大都市。
    - Guǎngzhōu shì Zhōngguó de nánfāng dà dūshì.
    - Guangzhou is a major metropolis in southern China.
  - 我昨天在广(廣)州参(參)加了一场(場)音乐会(樂會)，感受到了城市的魅力。
    - Wǒ zuótiān zài Guǎngzhōu cānjiāle yī chǎng yīnyuèhuì, gǎnshòu dào le chéngshì de mèilì.
    - I attended a concert in Guangzhou yesterday and experienced the charm of the city.
### 广(廣)州( ) → 广(廣)
- **traditional:** 廣
- **definition:** broad
- **pinyin:** guǎng
- **components:**
  - 宀
    - mián
    - roof
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with a roof, similar to 宀 (mián, "roof") ->
    - a building with three walls ->
    - shelter
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 广(廣) (guǎng, "shelter") visually represents a three-walled structure under a roof, conveying the concept of shelter or covering. It is closely related to the character 宀 (mián, "roof"), which includes four walls, indicating the structural nuance captured by ancient scribes.
  - **simplification:** 广(廣) was simplified by using the pictographic element alone, omitting the phonetic component 黃.
- **examples:**
  - 暴风骤(風驟)雨时(時)，山洞广(廣)可供人躲避。
    - Bào fēng zhòu yǔ shí, shān dòng guǎng kě gòng rén duǒ bì.
    - When the storm rages, the cave provides shelter.
  - 旅途中疲惫时(憊時)，老树(樹)下广给(廣給)予行人庇护(護)。
    - Lǚ tú zhōng pí bèi shí, lǎo shù xià guǎng jǐ yǔ xíng rén bì hù.
    - During a tiring journey, the shelter under the old tree gives travelers protection.
### 广(廣)州( ) → 广(廣) → 宀
- **definition:** roof
- **pinyin:** mián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**
  - 含有宀的汉(漢)字代表家的温(溫)暖。
    - Hán yǒu mián de hànzì dàibiǎo jiā de wēnnuǎn.
    - Chinese characters that include the radical '宀' represent the warmth of home.
  - 屋顶(頂)遮风挡(風擋)雨，家园(園)散发温(發溫)馨。
    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.
### 广(廣)州( ) → 州
- **definition:** state; region
- **pinyin:** zhōu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an islet in a river
  - **interpretation:** 州 (zhōu, "administrative division") was originally a pictogram representing a small piece of land or islet amidst water, illustrating the ancient practice of using distinct land areas as administrative divisions.
- **examples:**
  - 我计划参观几个(計劃參觀幾個)州。
    - Wǒ jìhuà cānguān jǐ gè zhōu.
    - I plan to visit several states.
  - 美国(國)的各州都有独(獨)特的风(風)景。
    - Měiguó de gè zhōu dōu yǒu dútè de fēngjǐng.
    - Every state in the United States has unique scenery.
  - 州政府负责(負責)管理地方事务(務)，政策由州长(長)制定。
    - Zhōu zhèngfǔ fùzé guǎnlǐ dìfāng shìwù, zhèngcè yóu zhōu zhǎng zhìdìng.
    - The state government is responsible for managing local affairs, and the policies are set by the governor.

## 加
---
## to increase; to add
### jiā
---
- **definition:** to increase; to add
- **pinyin:** jiā
- **components:**
  - 力
    - lì
    - strength
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 力 (lì, "strength") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") =
    - applying strength vocally ->
    - add
  - **interpretation:** The character 加 (jiā, "add") shows the idea of using strength in a vocal or pronounced way, suggesting an emphasis or increase, which aligns with the meaning of 'to add.'
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)加糖。
    - Qǐng jiā táng.
    - Please add sugar.
  - 厨师(廚師)在汤里(湯裡)加盐(鹽)，让(讓)味道更浓(濃)。
    - Chúshī zài tāng lǐ jiā yán, ràng wèidào gèng nóng.
    - The chef adds salt to the soup, making the flavor richer.
  - 他总(總)是加一点(點)努力，来(來)克服困难(難)。
    - Tā zǒngshì jiā yīdiǎn nǔlì, lái kèfú kùnnán.
    - He always adds a bit more effort to overcome difficulties.
### 加 → 力
- **definition:** strength
- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts either an arm bending out from the side of the body, or a wooden plough
  - **interpretation:** The character 力(lì, 'strength') visually represents physical power through the image of an arm or tool, emphasizing the fundamental concept of muscular force.
- **examples:**
  - 他用尽(盡)全力，赢(贏)得比赛(賽)。
    - Tā yòng jìn quánlì, yíng dé bǐsài.
    - He used all his strength to win the competition.
  - 他把力气(氣)用在学习(學習)上。
    - Tā bǎ lìqì yòng zài xuéxí shàng.
    - He applies his strength to his studies.
  - 面对(對)困难(難)，他毫不退缩(縮)，全力以赴。
    - Miànduì kùnnán, tā háo bù tuìsuō, quánlì yǐ fù.
    - Facing difficulties, he neither retreats nor gives up, but goes all out.
### 加 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张开(張開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.

## 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報)
---
## weather forecast
### tiānqì yùbào
---
- **traditional:** 天氣預報
- **definition:** weather forecast
- **pinyin:** tiānqì yùbào
- **components:**
  - 天氣
    - tiānqì
    - heaven; sky; air; atmosphere
  - 預報
    - yùbào
    - in advance; beforehand; report; announce
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 天 (tiān, "heaven; sky"), 氣 (qì, "air; atmosphere"), 預 (yù, "in advance; beforehand"), 報 (bào, "report; announce")
  - **interpretation:** The word 天氣預報 (tiānqì yùbào) combines the elements of the sky and atmosphere (天氣/天氣) with the concept of reporting or announcing in advance (預報/預報), which effectively communicates the idea of predicting and announcing the weather conditions ahead of time.
- **examples:**
  - 我每天早上看天气预报(氣預報)。
    - Wǒ měitiān zǎoshang kàn tiānqì yùbào.
    - I check the weather forecast every morning.
  - 电视(電視)上报(報)道天气预报(氣預報)，预(預)示着(著)大风(風)天气(氣)。
    - Diànshì shàng bàodào tiānqì yùbào, yùshìzhe dàfēng tiānqì.
    - The TV broadcasts the weather forecast, indicating strong winds.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天氣
- **definition:** heaven; sky; air; atmosphere
- **pinyin:** tiānqì
- **components:**
  - 天
    - tiān
    - heaven; sky
  - 氣
    - qì
    - air; atmosphere
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 天 (tiān, "heaven; sky") + 氣 (qì, "air; atmosphere") =
    - refers to the state of the atmosphere or 'weather'
  - **interpretation:** The word 天氣 (tiānqì, "weather") combines 天 (tiān, "heaven; sky") with 氣 (qì, "air; atmosphere") to describe the atmospheric conditions we experience. This concept connects the natural elements of the sky and atmosphere with weather patterns.
- **examples:**
  - 今天天氣很好。
    - Jīntiān tiānqì hěn hǎo.
    - The weather today is very good.
  - 我们(們)在公园(園)散步，享受宜人的天氣。
    - Wǒmen zài gōngyuán sànbù, xiǎngshòu yírén de tiānqì.
    - We take a walk in the park, enjoying the pleasant air.
  - 清晨的天氣凉(涼)爽，适(適)合跑步。
    - Qīngchén de tiānqì liángshuǎng, shìhé pǎobù.
    - The early morning weather is cool, perfect for running.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天氣 → 天
- **definition:** heaven; sky
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜幕降临(臨)，天边(邊)星光闪烁(閃爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈求天佑众(眾)生。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天氣 → 氣
- **definition:** air; atmosphere
- **pinyin:** qì
- **components:**
  - 气
    - qì
    - air
  - 米
    - mǐ
    - rice
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 气 (pronunciation) + Semantic: 米 ('rice') =
    - to give rice as a gift ->
    - borrowed for 'air, flow'
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 氣(qì, 'air') represented giving rice as a gift, reflecting physical exchange and transformation. Over time, it was borrowed to denote the concepts of 'air' and 'flow', abstractly related to the movement and circulation of gases.
  - **simplification:** The character 氣 was simplified to 气 by omitting the 米 (mǐ, 'rice') component, retaining only the phonetic element.
- **examples:**
  - 我们(們)呼吸着(著)新鲜(鮮)的气(氣)，迎接新的一天。
    - Wǒmen hūxīzhe xīnxiān de qì, yíngjiē xīn de yītiān.
    - We breathe in fresh air, welcoming a new day.
  - 空气温(氣溫)暖宜人。
    - Kōngqì wēnnuǎn yírén.
    - The air is pleasantly warm.
  - 大海的气(氣)，带着咸湿(帶著鹹濕)的味道。
    - Dàhǎi de qì, dàizhe xiánshī de wèidào.
    - The sea air carries a salty, humid scent.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天氣 → 氣 → 气(氣)
- **traditional:** 氣
- **definition:** air
- **pinyin:** qì
- **components:**
  - 三
    - sān
    - three
  - 乞
    - qǐ
    - beg
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Clouds flowing through the sky ->
    - altered to avoid confusion with 三 (sān, "three") ->
    - 乞 (qǐ, "beg") as a variant for phonetic borrowing
  - **interpretation:** The character 气(qì, "air") started as a pictogram representing clouds in the sky, which evolved to differentiate from the character for "three." Over time, 乞 was used as a variant for phonetic reasons, specifically for the meaning "to beg." The meanings 'air, flow' were later borrowed from 气.
- **examples:**
  - 房间里(間裡)的气(氣)很清新。
    - Fángjiān lǐ de qì hěn qīngxīn。
    - The air in the room is very fresh.
  - 打开(開)窗户(戶)，让(讓)新鲜(鮮)的气进来(氣進來)。
    - Dǎkāi chuānghù, ràng xīnxiān de qì jìnlái。
    - Open the window to let fresh air in.
  - 他深吸一口气(氣)，感觉(覺)心情舒畅(暢)。
    - Tā shēn xī yīkǒu qì, gǎnjué xīnqíng shūchàng。
    - He took a deep breath and felt his mood lift.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天氣 → 氣 → 气(氣) → 三
- **definition:** three
- **pinyin:** sān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 一 (yī, "one") triplicated ->
    - 三 (sān, "three")
  - **interpretation:** The character 三 (sān, "three") is an ideogram depicting the concept of the number three through the use of three parallel horizontal strokes. This straightforward representation makes it consistent with related numeric characters like 一 (yī, "one") and 二 (èr, "two").
- **examples:**
  - 今天我买(買)了三斤苹(蘋)果。
    - Jīntiān wǒ mǎi le sān jīn píngguǒ.
    - Today I bought three jin of apples.
  - 他有三支笔(筆)，我只想要其中一支。
    - Tā yǒu sān zhī bǐ, wǒ zhǐ xiǎng yào qízhōng yī zhī.
    - He has three pens, but I only want one of them.
  - 他们(們)吃了三碗面(麵)，觉(覺)得非常满(滿)意。
    - Tāmen chī le sān wǎn miàn, juéde fēicháng mǎnyì.
    - They ate three bowls of noodles and felt very satisfied.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天氣 → 氣 → 气(氣) → 乞
- **definition:** beg
- **pinyin:** qǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a person bending over with a bowl, resembling the act of begging.
  - **interpretation:** The character 乞 (qǐ, "beg") visually suggests the posture of a person soliciting aid or alms. This imagery supports its meaning of asking for or requesting something, often in a context of necessity.
- **examples:**
  - 他在街头(頭)乞讨(討)。
    - Tā zài jiētóu qǐtǎo.
    - He begs on the street.
  - 街头(頭)的乞丐请(請)求施舍(捨)。
    - Jiētóu de qǐgài qǐngqiú shīshě.
    - The beggar on the street asks for alms.
  - 他乞求雨露，期盼滋润(潤)大地。
    - Tā qǐqiú yǔlù, qīpàn zīrùn dàdì.
    - He begs for rainwater, hoping to nourish the earth.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 天氣 → 氣 → 米
- **definition:** rice
- **pinyin:** mǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts rice kernels ->
    - 米(mǐ, 'rice')
  - **interpretation:** The character 米(mǐ, 'rice') visually represents dehusked rice kernels to differentiate it from 粟. The horizontal stroke may symbolize a bamboo sieve, emphasizing the process of separating grains from their husks.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜欢(歡)吃米饭(飯)。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān chī mǐfàn.
    - I like to eat rice.
  - 她从农(從農)村带(帶)回一袋米，用来(來)煮饭(飯)。
    - Tā cóng nóngcūn dài huí yī dài mǐ, yòng lái zhǔ fàn.
    - She brought a bag of rice from the countryside to cook.
  - 市场(場)上有新米出售。
    - Shìchǎng shàng yǒu xīn mǐ chūshòu.
    - New rice is available in the market.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報
- **definition:** in advance; beforehand; report; announce
- **pinyin:** yùbào
- **components:**
  - 預
    - yù
    - in advance; beforehand
  - 報
    - bào
    - report; announce
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 預 (yù, "in advance; beforehand") + 報 (bào, "report; announce") together form a word that means to report or announce something in advance.
  - **interpretation:** The term 預報 (yùbào) combines the idea of doing something in advance, 預 (yù, "in advance"), with the act of reporting or announcing, 報 (bào, "report"). Typically, this refers to the action of forecasting or predicting future events, most commonly seen in weather forecasts.
- **examples:**
  - 气(氣)象部门(門)預報今天将(將)有暴雨。
    - Qìxiàng bùmén yùbào jīntiān jiāng yǒu bàoyǔ.
    - The meteorological department predicted that there would be heavy rain today.
  - 他们(們)預報会(會)提前出发(發)，所以大家做好准备(準備)。
    - Tāmen yùbào huì tíqián chūfā, suǒyǐ dàjiā zuòhǎo zhǔnbèi.
    - They announced that they would set off in advance, so everyone should get ready.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預
- **definition:** in advance; beforehand
- **pinyin:** yù
- **components:**
  - 予
    - yǔ
    - to give
  - 頁
    - yè
    - head
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 予 (yǔ, "to give") + Semantic: 頁 (yè, "head") =
    - Phono-semantic compound indicating something prepared in advance
  - **interpretation:** The character 預(yù) combines 予 (yǔ, "to give") as the phonetic component and 頁 (yè, "head") as the semantic component, illustrating the concept of anticipating or preparing something ahead of time, perhaps metaphorically suggesting preparation is 'given' thought.
  - **simplification:** 預 is simplified to 预(預) by replacing the full form of 頁 with the simpler 预, maintaining the overall meaning while reducing the number of strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他預习(習)了明天的课(課)。
    - Tā yùxí le míngtiān de kè.
    - He reviewed tomorrow's lesson in advance.
  - 我们预(們預)先安排了旅行，准备(準備)了所有用品。
    - Wǒmen yùxiān ānpái le lǚxíng, zhǔnbèi le suǒyǒu yòngpǐn.
    - We arranged the trip in advance and prepared all the supplies.
  - 我提前預算了费(費)用，以防万(萬)一。
    - Wǒ tíqián yùsuàn le fèiyòng, yǐ fáng wànyī.
    - I budgeted the expenses in advance just in case.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 予
- **definition:** to give
- **pinyin:** yǔ
- **components:**
  - 呂
    - lǚ
    - spine
  - 亅
    - jué
    - hook
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Jiajie
  - **description:**
    - Originally written as 呂 (lǚ, "spine") for phonetic purposes ->
    - borrowed for "give" and "I" ->
    - distinguishing 亅 (jué, "hook") added at the bottom ->
    - stylized to final form 予 (yǔ, "give")
  - **interpretation:** The character 予 (yǔ, "give") was adapted from 呂 (lǚ, "spine") due to phonetic similarity. The addition of 亅 (jué, "hook") helped set it apart visually, leading to the modern form.
- **examples:**
  - 他予我一本书(書)。
    - Tā yǔ wǒ yī běn shū.
    - He gave me a book.
  - 老师(師)予以指导(導)，学(學)生表示感谢(謝)。
    - Lǎoshī yǔyǐ zhǐdǎo, xuéshēng biǎoshì gǎnxiè.
    - The teacher provided guidance and the students expressed their gratitude.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 予 → 呂
- **definition:** spine
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **components:**
  - 鋁
    - lǚ
    - ingot
  - 膂
    - lǚ
    - spine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two blocks of metal ->
    - original form of 鋁 (lǚ, 'ingot') ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 膂 (lǚ, 'spine') and 呂 (lǚ, 'music notes')
  - **interpretation:** Initially a pictogram illustrating two disconnected metal blocks, the character 呂 (lǚ, 'two blocks of metal') was later adapted by connecting the blocks, becoming stylized as it was repurposed for various meanings including 'spine' and 'music notes'.
  - **simplification:** 呂 was adapted into 呂(吕) as a simplified form without altering the meaning, simplifying the lines to produce a more cursive appearance.
- **examples:**
  - 工匠将(將)呂打造成精美的装饰(裝飾)品。
    - Gōngjiàng jiāng Lǚ dǎzào chéng jīngměi de zhuāngshìpǐn.
    - The artisan forged the two blocks of metal into an exquisite ornament.
  - 考古学(學)家在古墓中发现(發現)了呂。
    - Kǎogǔ xuéjiā zài gǔmù zhōng fāxiànle Lǚ.
    - The archaeologist discovered the two blocks of metal in the ancient tomb.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 予 → 呂 → 鋁
- **definition:** ingot
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **components:**
  - 金
    - jīn
    - metal
  - 慮
    - lǜ
    - consider
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 金 (jīn, "metal; gold") + phonetic 慮 (lǜ) =
    - related to metal properties ->
    - ingot
  - **interpretation:** 鋁(lǚ) ("ingot") combines 金 to indicate association with metal and 慮 as a phonetic component, suggesting the importance of careful consideration in metallurgy.
- **examples:**
  - 工厂里(廠裡)熔化的铝经过(鋁經過)快速冷却后(卻後)，凝固成锭(錠)形状(狀)。
    - Gōngchǎng lǐ rónghuà de lǚ jīngguò kuàisù lěngquè hòu, nínggù chéng dìng xíngzhuàng.
    - In the factory, the melted aluminum quickly cooled and solidified into ingot shapes.
  - 冶炼(煉)工匠精心铸(鑄)造铝为(鋁為)高质(質)量锭(錠)。
    - Yěliàn gōngjiàng jīngxīn zhùzào lǚ wèi gāo zhìliàng dìng.
    - The metallurgists meticulously cast the aluminum into high-quality ingots.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 予 → 呂 → 膂
- **definition:** spine
- **pinyin:** lǚ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form
  - **description:** 膂 is a variant form of 呂 (lǚ, "spine")
  - **interpretation:** Originating as a pictogram depicting two disconnected blocks, 呂 was initially associated with metal and later reinterpreted as vertebrae through the addition of a connecting line, representing 9 (lǚ, "spine"). The character 呂 was phonetically borrowed for this meaning, while 膂 emphasizes its anatomical sense with the addition of the 肉 (ròu, "flesh") radical.
- **examples:**
  - 他的膂十分强(強)健。
    - Tā de lǚ shífēn qiángjiàn.
    - His spine is very strong.
  - 练习(練習)瑜伽可以增强(強)膂，保持身体(體)健康。
    - Liànxí yújiā kěyǐ zēngqiáng lǚ, bǎochí shēntǐ jiànkāng.
    - Practicing yoga can strengthen the spine, helping to maintain a healthy body.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 予 → 亅
- **definition:** hook
- **pinyin:** jué
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a simple vertical line with a slight hook at the bottom
  - **interpretation:** 亅 (jué, "hook") is a pictogram representing a hook or bent line, emphasizing the hooked end. It is used as a component in other characters.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 頁
- **definition:** head
- **pinyin:** yè
- **components:**
  - 首
    - shǒu
    - head
  - 卩
    - jié
    - kneeling person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 首 (shǒu, "head") + 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") =
    - head of a kneeling person ->
    - emphasis on "head" ->
    - later used for "page"
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting the head of a kneeling person, 頁(yè) was adapted to signify 'page' by association with leaves (葉). While its original sense of 'head' is retained in some radicals, its contemporary meaning as 'page' is more commonly recognized.
  - **simplification:** 頁 was simplified by adopting the cursive script version, resulting in 页. This process focused on reducing the complexity of the character while maintaining its phonetic resemblance.
- **examples:**
  - 书(書)的第一页(頁)上印有精美的插图(圖)。
    - Shū de dì yī yè shàng yìn yǒu jīng měi de chā tú.
    - The first page of the book is printed with exquisite illustrations.
  - 她认(認)真阅读(閱讀)每一頁，体会(體會)作者的用意。
    - Tā rèn zhēn yuè dú měi yī yè, tǐ huì zuò zhě de yòng yì.
    - She carefully reads every page to appreciate the author's intentions.
  - 翻开这几(開這幾)頁，你将发现(將發現)一个(個)新世界。
    - Fān kāi zhè jǐ yè, nǐ jiāng fā xiàn yī gè xīn shì jiè.
    - Turn over these pages, and you will discover a new world.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 頁 → 首
- **definition:** head
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a head with the stylized representation of eyes and hair
  - **interpretation:** The character 首 (shǒu, 'head') depicts a head, with the top portion representing hair and a central line suggesting a facial feature, effectively conveying the concept of a head.
- **examples:**
  - 他昂首挺胸走上领奖(領獎)台。
    - Tā áng shǒu tǐng xiōng zǒu shàng lǐng jiǎng tái.
    - He walked onto the podium with his head held high.
  - 受伤后(傷後)，他低下首表示谦逊(謙遜)。
    - Shòu shāng hòu, tā dī xià shǒu biǎo shì qiān xùn.
    - After being injured, he lowered his head to show humility.
  - 他被选为(選為)公司的首席执(執)行官。
    - Tā bèi xuǎn wéi gōng sī de shǒu xí zhí xíng guān.
    - He was elected as the company's chief executive officer.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 預 → 頁 → 卩
- **definition:** kneeling person
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a kneeling person from sideview
  - **interpretation:** The character 卩 (jié, "kneeling person") is a simple pictogram showing the silhouette of a person kneeling. It is unrelated to other kneeling or similar figures in different contexts such as 欠 (qiàn, "yawn") where the mouth is open, or 女 (nǚ, "woman") where the figure represents a female. Its form is solely based on the posture of kneeling.
- **examples:**
  - 那位卩正虔诚(誠)祈祷(禱)。
    - Nà wèi jié zhèng qiánchéng qídǎo.
    - That kneeling person is praying devoutly.
  - 礼仪师(禮儀師)指出，卩代表谦(謙)卑与(與)敬意。
    - Lǐyí shī zhǐchū, jié dàibiǎo qiānbēi yǔ jìngyì.
    - The ritual master pointed out that the kneeling person represents humility and respect.
  - 在庄严仪(莊嚴儀)式中，卩象征着内(徵著內)心的虔敬。
    - Zài zhuāngyán yíshì zhōng, jié xiàngzhēngzhe nèixīn de qiánjìng.
    - In the solemn ceremony, the kneeling figure symbolizes inner devotion.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 報
- **definition:** report; announce
- **pinyin:** bào
- **components:**
  - 㚔
    - n/a
    - handcuffs
  - 𠬝
    - n/a
    - to subdue
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 㚔 (handcuffs) + 𠬝 (to subdue) =
    - to convict or declare guilty ->
    - report; announce
  - **interpretation:** The character 報(bào) conveys the idea of delivering a verdict or making an official announcement, stemming from the imagery of handcuffs and subdual, which symbolize an authoritative declaration of guilt.
  - **simplification:** 報 was simplified to 报 through sound-alike replacement with 押 (yā, "press"), retaining the idea of administering announcements but using the simpler form.
- **examples:**
  - 记(記)者報最新消息。
    - Jìzhě bào zuìxīn xiāoxī.
    - The reporter reported the latest news.
  - 听(聽)到火警铃声(鈴聲)，他立刻報警。
    - Tīngdào huǒjǐng língshēng, tā lìkè bào jǐng.
    - Hearing the fire alarm, he immediately called the police.
  - 校长(長)報考试(試)成绩(績)。
    - Xiàozhǎng bào kǎoshì chéngjì.
    - The principal reported the exam results.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 報 → 㚔
- **definition:** handcuffs
- **pinyin:** n/a
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts handcuffs
  - **interpretation:** The character 㚔 is a pictogram representing handcuffs, illustrating the shape of restraints used on wrists. It visually captures the concept of confinement or restriction.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 報 → 𠬝
- **definition:** to subdue
- **pinyin:** n/a
- **components:**
  - 服
    - fú
    - to serve
  - 凡
    - fán
    - tray
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠬝 depicts a form related to 服 (fú, "to serve") ->
    - 凡 (fán, "tray") was added for semantic meaning, evolving phonetics over time
  - **interpretation:** Originally a pictogram, 𠬝 served as the form for 服 (fú, "to serve") meaning 'to subdue.' The character 凡 was later added for its semantic layer, but over time it was corrupted into other forms like 舟 (zhōu, "boat") and 月 (yuè, "moon"), which influenced the character's development.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 報 → 𠬝 → 服
- **definition:** to serve
- **pinyin:** fú
- **components:**
  - 凡
    - fán
    - tray
  - 舟
    - zhōu
    - boat
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𠬝 (original pictogram depicting 'to subdue') ->
    - 凡 (fán, 'tray') added as semantic ->
    - 凡 corrupted into 舟 (zhōu, 'boat') and then 月 (yuè, 'moon') ->
    - final form 服 (fú, 'serve')
  - **interpretation:** The character 服 (fú, 'serve') originates from a pictogram 𠬝 showing subjugation, conveying the idea of 'serving or obeying.' The addition of 凡 changes its visual into something resembling 舟 and then 月, enhancing the character's complexity without altering its core semantic value.
- **examples:**
  - 士兵服从(從)命令，保护(護)人民。
    - Shìbīng fúcóng mìnglìng, bǎohù rénmín.
    - The soldiers obey orders and protect the people.
  - 他穿上军(軍)服，准备(準備)出发(發)。
    - Tā chuān shàng jūnfú, zhǔnbèi chūfā.
    - He puts on his military uniform and gets ready to depart.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 報 → 𠬝 → 服 → 凡
- **definition:** tray
- **pinyin:** fán
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a plate or flat dish ->
    - borrowed for abstract meanings ->
    - unrelated to 几(幾) (jī, 'small table')
  - **interpretation:** 凡 (fán, 'ordinary') originally depicted a flat dish or plate. Over time, it expanded to encompass broader abstract meanings and is unrelated to the character 几(幾) which represents a small table.
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)平凡的人。
    - tā shì gè píngfán de rén.
    - He is an ordinary person.
  - 凡人都可能犯错(錯)，从错误(從錯誤)中成长(長)。
    - fán rén dōu kěnéng fàncuò, cóng cuòwù zhōng chéngzhǎng.
    - Ordinary people may make mistakes, and grow from them.
  - 他凡去旅行，总(總)能发现(發現)新的风(風)景。
    - tā fán qù lǚxíng, zǒng néng fāxiàn xīn de fēngjǐng.
    - Whenever he travels, he always discovers new sceneries.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 報 → 𠬝 → 服 → 舟
- **definition:** boat
- **pinyin:** zhōu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a boat
  - **interpretation:** The character 舟 (zhōu, "boat") visually represents the outline of a boat, reflecting its function and form.
- **examples:**
  - 小舟在湖中摇(搖)曳。
    - Xiǎo zhōu zài hú zhōng yáoyè.
    - The small boat sways on the lake.
  - 他驾着(駕著)一只(隻)小舟，穿过雾气弥(過霧氣彌)漫的河面。
    - Tā jiàzhe yī zhōu, chuānguò wùqì mímàn de hémiàn.
    - He steers a small boat, crossing a river shrouded in mist.
  - 清晨时(時)分舟载(載)行人，穿过(過)古镇(鎮)河流。
    - Qīngchén shífèn zhōu zài xíngrén, chuānguò gǔzhèn héliú.
    - In the early morning, the boat carries passengers as it passes through the ancient town's river.
### 天( )气(氣)预(預)报(報) → 預報 → 報 → 𠬝 → 服 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂着(掛著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们赏(們賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.

## 晴天
---
## sunny day; clear sky
### qíngtiān
---
- **definition:** sunny day; clear sky
- **pinyin:** qíngtiān
- **components:**
  - 晴
    - qíng
    - clear; fine [weather]
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky; day
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 晴 (qíng, "clear; fine [weather]") + 天 (tiān, "sky; day") =
    - a day with clear sky and good weather.
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 晴 (qíng, "clear; fine [weather]") and 天 (tiān, "sky; day") conveys the idea of a day where the sky is clear and the weather is favorable. This aligns with the term 'sunny day' or 'clear sky,' describing conditions without clouds or rain, highlighting pleasant weather.
- **examples:**
  - 今天是个(個)晴天。
    - Jīntiān shì gè qíngtiān。
    - Today is a sunny day.
  - 每当(當)遇到晴天，心情就特别(別)好。
    - Měi dāng yù dào qíngtiān, xīnqíng jiù tèbié hǎo。
    - Whenever it's a sunny day, the mood becomes especially pleasant.
  - 晴天时(時)，小鸟(鳥)在枝头(頭)歌唱。
    - Qíngtiān shí, xiǎo niǎo zài zhītóu gēchàng。
    - On a sunny day, little birds sing on the branches.
### 晴天 → 晴
- **definition:** clear; fine [weather]
- **pinyin:** qíng
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 青
    - qīng
    - blue-green
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, "sun") + 青 (qīng, phonetic) =
    - sun shining brightly ->
    - clear, fine (weather)
  - **interpretation:** 晴 (qíng) combines the semantic element 日 (rì, "sun"), representing sunlight, with the phonetic 青 (qīng), suggesting clarity or brightness. Together, they convey the notion of clear, fine weather when the sun is unobstructed, which aligns with the character's meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 今天天气(氣)晴，万(萬)里无云(無雲)。
    - Jīntiān tiānqì qíng, wànlǐ wú yún.
    - Today's weather is clear, with not a cloud in sight.
  - 晴天适(適)合出游(遊)。
    - Qíngtiān shìhé chūyóu.
    - Clear weather is perfect for traveling.
  - 经过阴(經過陰)雨，现(現)已转(轉)晴。
    - Jīngguò yīnyǔ, xiàn yǐ zhuǎn qíng.
    - After days of rain, the weather has turned clear.
### 晴天 → 晴 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来临时(來臨時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒满(灑滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
### 晴天 → 晴 → 青
- **definition:** blue-green
- **pinyin:** qīng
- **components:**
  - 生
    - shēng
    - growth
  - 井
    - jǐng
    - well
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 生 (shēng, "growth") + Phonetic: 井 (jǐng, "well") =
    - combined phonetics ->
    - original meaning of "color of growing plants" ->
    - modern meaning "green"
  - **interpretation:** The character 青(qīng) originally combined phonetic elements to convey the idea of 'the color of growing plants,' associating it with green due to its relation to plant life. Over time, this evolved into its current meaning of 'green.'
  - **simplification:** The second-round simplified form retained the calligraphic appearance, refining the top component 龶 to modernize the character while preserving its semantic elements.
- **examples:**
  - 那件青衫展现(現)出独(獨)特韵(韻)味。
    - nà jiàn qīng shān zhǎn xiàn chū dú tè yùn wèi。
    - That green garment displays a unique charm.
  - 他骑着(騎著)青马奔驰(馬馳騁)在草原上。
    - tā qí zhe qīng mǎ chì chěng zài cǎo yuán shàng。
    - He rides a green horse galloping on the grassland.
  - 湖水映着(著)青天，江畔伫(佇)立青松。
    - hú shuǐ yìng zhe qīng tiān, jiāng pàn zhù lì qīng sōng。
    - The lake reflects the blue sky, and by the river the green pines stand tall.
### 晴天 → 晴 → 青 → 生
- **definition:** growth
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生命是一场(場)美丽(麗)的旅程。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他在战场(戰場)上奋(奮)力生存。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家餐厅(廳)的生鱼(魚)片非常新鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
### 晴天 → 晴 → 青 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润后(潤後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
### 晴天 → 晴 → 青 → 井
- **definition:** well
- **pinyin:** jǐng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a grid symbolizing a well's structure
  - **interpretation:** The character 井 (jǐng, "well") visually represents the framework or grid of wooden or stone beams that would make up the top view of a traditional well, highlighting its function and design.
- **examples:**
  - 村口有一口老井。
    - Cūnkǒu yǒuyī kǒu lǎo jǐng.
    - There is an old well at the village entrance.
  - 夏天酷热时(熱時)，井水带来阵阵凉(帶來陣陣涼)意。
    - Xiàtiān kùrè shí, jǐng shuǐ dàilái zhèn zhèn liángyì.
    - In the scorching summer, well water brings a refreshing coolness.
### 晴天 → 天
- **definition:** sky; day
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜幕降临(臨)，天边(邊)星光闪烁(閃爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈求天佑众(眾)生。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.

## 晴天
### qíngtiān
---
## sunny day; clear sky

## 中( )国(國)民( )航( )
---
## Civil Aviation Administration of China (CAAC)
### Zhōngguó Mínháng
---
- **traditional:** 中國民航
- **definition:** Civil Aviation Administration of China (CAAC)
- **pinyin:** Zhōngguó Mínháng
- **components:**
  - 中
    - zhōng
    - middle
  - 國
    - guó
    - country
  - 民
    - mín
    - people; civil
  - 航
    - háng
    - navigation; aviation
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 中 (zhōng, "middle") + 國 (guó, "country") =
    - 中國 (zhōngguó, "China"); 民 (mín, "people; civil") + 航 (háng, "navigation; aviation") =
    - 民航 (mínháng, "civil aviation")
  - **interpretation:** 中國 (zhōngguó, "China") refers to the country, while 民航 (mínháng, "civil aviation") denotes the sector focused on civilian air transportation. Combined, 中國民航 refers to the Civil Aviation Administration of China, the national body overseeing civil aviation in the country.
- **examples:**
  - 中国(國)民航监(監)管严(嚴)格。
    - Zhōngguó Mínháng jiānguǎn yángé.
    - The Civil Aviation Administration of China enforces strict oversight.
  - 中国(國)民航安全记录(記錄)良好，促进国际(進國際)合作。
    - Zhōngguó Mínháng ānquán jìlù liánghǎo, cùjìn guójì hézuò.
    - The CAAC has a good safety record, fostering international cooperation.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 中
- **definition:** middle
- **pinyin:** zhōng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an arrow piercing through the center of a target
  - **interpretation:** The character 中 (zhōng, "middle") visually represents an arrow passing through the central point of a target, illustrating the concept of 'center' or 'middle' effectively. This visual imagery is straightforward and memorable, corresponding closely with its meaning of being at the center or middle of something.
- **examples:**
  - 他站在道路中，看着远(著遠)方。
    - tā zhàn zài dàolù zhōng, kànzhe yuǎnfāng.
    - He stands in the middle of the road, gazing into the distance.
  - 房间(間)正中，挂着(掛著)一幅名画(畫)。
    - fángjiān zhèng zhōng, guàzhe yī fú mínghuà.
    - A famous painting hangs in the exact center of the room.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國
- **definition:** country
- **pinyin:** guó
- **components:**
  - 囗
    - wéi
    - closure
  - 或
    - huò
    - or
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 囗 (wéi, "closure") + phonetic 或 (huò, "or") ->
    - enclosed area signifying a state or country
  - **interpretation:** The character 國 (guó, "country") combines the idea of an enclosed space from 囗 (wéi, "closure") with the phonetic component 或 (huò, "or"), suggesting a defined and protected area, aligning with the concept of a country or state.
  - **simplification:** The simplified character 国(國) uses 玉 (yù, "jade") as a mnemonic for wealth within an enclosure, dropping the component 或 (huò, "or") for simplicity.
- **examples:**
  - 这个国(這個國)有着独(著獨)特魅力。
    - Zhège guó yǒuzhe dútè mèilì.
    - This country has a unique charm.
  - 许(許)多人热爱国(熱愛國)文化，努力建设国(設國)的美好明天。
    - Xǔduō rén rè'ài guó wénhuà, nǔlì jiànshè guó de měihǎo míngtiān.
    - Many people cherish their country's culture and strive to build a better future.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國 → 囗
- **definition:** closure
- **pinyin:** wéi
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an enclosure
  - **interpretation:** The character 囗 (wéi, 'enclosure') is a pictogram representing a square or rectangular enclosure, emblematic of walls or boundaries. It visually reflects a basic enclosed area delineated by straight lines.
- **examples:**
  - 博物馆(館)外有坚(堅)固的囗，保护着历(護著歷)史文物。
    - Bówùguǎn wài yǒu jiāngù de wéi, bǎohùzhe lìshǐ wénwù.
    - Outside the museum, a sturdy enclosure protects historical artifacts.
  - 古城外围(圍)的囗，确(確)保了居民的安全。
    - Gǔchéng wàiwéi de wéi, quèbǎole jūmín de ānquán.
    - The ancient city's enclosure ensures the residents' safety.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國 → 或
- **definition:** or
- **pinyin:** huò
- **components:**
  - 戈
    - gē
    - spear
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 戈 (gē, "spear") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - a person using a spear with an open mouth ->
    - uncertain decision or possibility ->
    - final meaning 'or; maybe'
  - **interpretation:** The character combines a depiction of a weapon with a mouth, suggesting someone deliberating verbally while holding a spear, thus conveying uncertainty or consideration between options.
- **examples:**
  - 你可以挑选红(選紅)色，或蓝(藍)色。
    - nǐ kěyǐ tiāoxuǎn hóngsè, huò lán sè.
    - You can choose red, or blue.
  - 他今天到达(達)，或明天再来(來)。
    - tā jīntiān dàodá, huò míngtiān zài lái.
    - He arrives today, or comes again tomorrow.
  - 午餐时(時)，你可选择面条(選擇麵條)，或米饭(飯)？
    - wǔcān shí, nǐ kě xuǎnzé miàntiáo, huò mǐfàn?
    - At lunch, you may choose noodles, or rice?
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國 → 或 → 戈
- **definition:** spear
- **pinyin:** gē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a spear or halberd, a type of weapon
  - **interpretation:** The character 戈(gē, 'spear') visually represents a spear or halberd, highlighting its function and importance as a weapon in ancient Chinese warfare.
- **examples:**
  - 古代战(戰)士持戈，勇闯敌营(闖敵營)。
    - Gǔdài zhànshì chí gē, yǒng chuǎng dí yíng.
    - Ancient warriors wielded the spear, bravely attacking the enemy camp.
  - 博物馆(館)珍藏古兵器，展厅陈(廳陳)列戈。
    - Bówùguǎn zhēncáng gǔ bīngqì, zhǎntīng chénliè gē.
    - The museum preserves ancient weapons, and the exhibition hall displays a spear.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國 → 或 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张开(張開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 國 → 或 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个苹(個蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只鸟(隻鳥)，飞进(飛進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 民
- **definition:** people; civil
- **pinyin:** mín
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an eye stabbed by a needle, symbolizing oppression of the people ->
    - people
  - **interpretation:** The character 民 (mín, 'people') originally depicted an eye being pierced by a tool, a metaphor for the suffering and experiences of the common people. This imagery evolved to represent the broader concept of the populace.
- **examples:**
  - 勤劳(勞)的民，构(構)成国(國)家的支柱。
    - Qínláo de mín, gòuchéng guójiā de zhīzhù.
    - Hardworking people form the backbone of the nation.
  - 民是国(國)家不可忽视(視)的力量。
    - Mín shì guójiā bùkě hūshì de lìliàng.
    - The people are an indispensable force in the country.
  - 民聚沙成塔。
    - Mín jù shā chéng tǎ.
    - People can achieve great feats through unity.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 航
- **definition:** navigation; aviation
- **pinyin:** háng
- **components:**
  - 舟
    - zhōu
    - boat
  - 亢
    - kàng
    - high
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 舟 (zhōu, "boat") + 亢 (kàng, "high") =
    - vessel-related concept with sound from phonetic ->
    - navigation or aviation
  - **interpretation:** The character 航 combines the semantic 舟 (zhōu, "boat"), indicating its association with boats or vessels, and the phonetic 亢 (kàng), which contributes to its pronunciation, thus relating to activities involving navigation or aviation.
- **examples:**
  - 飞机(飛機)在蓝(藍)天中航行。
    - Fēijī zài lántiān zhōng hángxíng.
    - The airplane navigates in the blue sky.
  - 古代水手依靠星辰航向，开启远(開啟遠)航梦(夢)想。
    - Gǔdài shuǐshǒu yīkào xīngchén hángxiàng, kāiqǐ yuǎn háng mèngxiǎng.
    - Ancient sailors relied on the stars for navigation and set off on dreams of long voyages.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 航 → 舟
- **definition:** boat
- **pinyin:** zhōu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a boat
  - **interpretation:** The character 舟 (zhōu, "boat") visually represents the outline of a boat, reflecting its function and form.
- **examples:**
  - 小舟在湖中摇(搖)曳。
    - Xiǎo zhōu zài hú zhōng yáoyè.
    - The small boat sways on the lake.
  - 他驾着(駕著)一只(隻)小舟，穿过雾气弥(過霧氣彌)漫的河面。
    - Tā jiàzhe yī zhōu, chuānguò wùqì mímàn de hémiàn.
    - He steers a small boat, crossing a river shrouded in mist.
  - 清晨时(時)分舟载(載)行人，穿过(過)古镇(鎮)河流。
    - Qīngchén shífèn zhōu zài xíngrén, chuānguò gǔzhèn héliú.
    - In the early morning, the boat carries passengers as it passes through the ancient town's river.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 航 → 亢
- **definition:** high
- **pinyin:** kàng
- **components:**
  - 二
    - èr
    - two
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 二 (èr, "two") above 人 (rén, "person") =
    - person lifting something high
  - **interpretation:** The character 亢 (kàng, "high") visually represents a person standing with arms raised, symbolizing the idea of lifting or being elevated. The combination of two horizontal strokes above a person conveys the notion of height or reaching upwards.
- **examples:**
  - 他的情绪(緒)亢奋(奮)。
    - tā de qíngxù kàng fèn。
    - His mood is highly excited.
  - 山峰高耸(聳)，气势(氣勢)亢然。
    - shānfēng gāosǒng, qìshì kàng rán。
    - The mountains tower high, and their momentum is exalted.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 航 → 亢 → 二
- **definition:** two
- **pinyin:** èr
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts two parallel strokes ->
    - represents the number two
  - **interpretation:** The character 二 (èr, "two") consists of two horizontal lines that visually represent the concept of 'two'. This method of using parallel strokes to denote numbers is a straightforward representation of quantity, similar to how 一 (yī, "one") represents 'one' and 三 (sān, "three") represents 'three'.
- **examples:**
  - 我有二支笔(筆)。
    - Wǒ yǒu èr zhī bǐ.
    - I have two pens.
  - 他买(買)了二个苹(個蘋)果，我们(們)一起分享。
    - Tā mǎi le èr gè píngguǒ, wǒmen yīqǐ fēnxiǎng.
    - He bought two apples, and we shared them together.
### 中( )国(國)民( )航( ) → 航 → 亢 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡献(貢獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵获(靈獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.

## 起( )飞(飛)
---
## to take off
### qǐfēi
---
- **traditional:** 起飛
- **definition:** to take off
- **pinyin:** qǐfēi
- **components:**
  - 起
    - qǐ
    - rise; initiate; begin; get up
  - 飛
    - fēi
    - fly; flutter; hover; rush
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 起 (qǐ, "rise") + 飛 (fēi, "fly") =
    - rise up to fly ->
    - take off
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 起 (qǐ, "rise") and 飛 (fēi, "fly") conveys the action of an aircraft lifting off the ground to begin flying. This is a straightforward and literal representation of the concept of taking off.
- **examples:**
  - 飞机(飛機)起飞(飛)。
    - Fēijī qǐfēi.
    - The airplane takes off.
  - 飞机(飛機)在跑道上加速，很快起飞(飛)。
    - Fēijī zài pǎodào shàng jiāsù, hěn kuài qǐfēi.
    - The airplane accelerates on the runway, then takes off quickly.
  - 准备(準備)完毕(畢)，飞机(飛機)起飞(飛)。
    - Zhǔnbèi wánbì, fēijī qǐfēi.
    - After getting ready, the airplane takes off.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起
- **definition:** rise; initiate; begin; get up
- **pinyin:** qǐ
- **components:**
  - 走
    - zǒu
    - walk
  - 巳
    - sì
    - sixth terrestrial branch
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 走 (zǒu, "walk") + phonetic: 巳 (sì, "sixth terrestrial branch") =
    - implying movement or ascent ->
    - rise, begin
  - **interpretation:** The character 起 (qǐ, "rise") combines 走 (zǒu, "walk"), indicating motion or activity, with 巳 (sì, "sixth terrestrial branch"), contributing the phonetic element. This combination intuitively represents the concept of rising or beginning.
- **examples:**
  - 我早上起床。
    - Wǒ zǎoshang qǐ chuáng.
    - I get up in the morning.
  - 太阳(陽)升起时(時)，世界变(變)得明亮。
    - Tàiyáng shēng qǐ shí, shìjiè biàn dé míngliàng.
    - When the sun rises, the world becomes bright.
  - 他鼓起勇气(氣)，面对(對)挑战(戰)。
    - Tā gǔ qǐ yǒngqì, miànduì tiǎozhàn.
    - He mustered his courage to face the challenges.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** zǒu
- **components:**
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 夭
    - yāo
    - young
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 龰
    - yuè
    - walking
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Running man (original depiction) + 止 (zhǐ, "foot") added later ->
    - top 夭 (yāo, "young") simplified to 土 (tǔ, "earth"), bottom stylized as 龰 ->
    - modern 走
  - **interpretation:** The character originally depicted a man running, with an added foot to emphasize movement. Over time, elements like the top 夭 were simplified to 土, and the bottom was stylized to 龰, although they are unrelated to the original meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 看到前方火光时(時)，他急忙走向安全地带(帶)。
    - Kàndào qiánfāng huǒguāng shí, tā jímáng zǒu xiàng ānquán dìdài.
    - When he saw the firelight ahead, he hurriedly ran toward safety.
  - 比赛开(賽開)始后(後)，选(選)手们奋(們奮)力走向终点(終點)。
    - Bǐsài kāishǐ hòu, xuǎnshǒu men fènlì zǒu xiàng zhōngdiǎn.
    - After the race began, the contestants ran towards the finish line.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静养(靜養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 足
    - zú
    - foot
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - stop
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 足 (zú, "foot") + 止 (zhǐ, "stop") =
    - semantic: foot + phonetic: stop ->
    - toe
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 足 (zú, "foot") as the semantic indicator and 止 (zhǐ, "stop") as the phonetic component to represent the idea of a 'toe,' which is a part of the foot.
- **examples:**
  - 他的趾因寒冷而僵硬了。
    - tā de zhǐ yīn hánlěng ér jiāngyìng le.
    - His toe became stiff due to the cold.
  - 我走路时(時)，不小心扭到了趾。
    - wǒ zǒulù shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ dào le zhǐ.
    - While I was walking, I accidentally twisted my toe.
  - 古代剑(劍)客战斗时(戰鬥時)，常因疏忽伤(傷)及趾。
    - gǔdài jiànkè zhàndòu shí, cháng yīn shūhū shāng jí zhǐ.
    - Ancient swordsmen often injured their toes due to carelessness during battles.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 趾 → 足
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zú
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a leg ->
    - originally depicted as ⽦ ->
    - represents 'foot'
  - **interpretation:** The character 足(zú, 'foot') is a pictographic representation of a human leg, which directly portrays the concept of a 'foot'. The pictographic origin emphasizes its fundamental meaning in the language.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤后(傷後)，他的足不能动(動)。
    - tā shòushāng hòu, tā de zú bù néng dòng。
    - After he was injured, his foot couldn't move.
  - 小明打球时(時)，不小心扭伤(傷)了足。
    - xiǎo míng dǎ qiú shí, bù xiǎoxīn niǔ shāng le zú。
    - When Xiaoming was playing ball, he accidentally twisted his foot.
  - 我每天锻炼(鍛鍊)足部。
    - wǒ měitiān duànliàn zúbù。
    - I exercise my foot muscles every day.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 龰
- **definition:** stylized feet
- **pinyin:** yù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a stylized foot with three toes ->
    - derivative form of 止 (zhǐ, "foot") ->
    - represented as 龰(yù)
  - **interpretation:** 龰(yù) visually represents a stylized foot with three toes, embodying its original meaning as 'foot'. This aligns with the depiction of footprints pointing up in early script forms, distinct from similar characters like 夊 and 夂, which depict feet with a downward orientation.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 止 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈妈牵着(媽媽牽著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带给(帶給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 夭
- **definition:** young
- **pinyin:** yāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a figure leaning forward, presumably running ->
    - energetic, young
  - **interpretation:** The character 夭(yāo) ("young") visually represents someone leaning forward in a motion that suggests energy and vitality associated with youthfulness. This imagery aligns with the concept of being lively or young.
- **examples:**
  - 他还夭，意气风发(氣風發)。
    - Tā hái yāo, yìqì fēngfā。
    - He is still young, full of youthful vigor.
  - 小女孩还夭，充满无(滿無)限活力。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái hái yāo, chōngmǎn wúxiàn huólì。
    - The little girl is still young, filled with boundless energy.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 走 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 起 → 巳
- **definition:** sixth terrestrial branch
- **pinyin:** sì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a fetus or snake.
  - **interpretation:** The character 巳(sì, "fetus") likely represents the shape of a fetus curled in the womb or possibly the sinuous form of a snake. This ambiguity is due to its pictographic origin, imitating the curves and forms seen in nature.
- **examples:**
  - 那小小的巳在温(溫)暖的子宫(宮)中悄然成长(長)。
    - Nà xiǎoxiǎo de sì zài wēnnuǎn de zǐgōng zhōng qiǎorán chéngzhǎng.
    - The tiny fetus is growing quietly in the warm womb.
  - 医(醫)生发现(發現)巳异(異)常，提醒家长(長)早期注意。
    - Yīshēng fāxiàn sì yìcháng, tíxǐng jiāzhǎng zǎoqī zhùyì.
    - The doctor found an abnormality in the fetus and urged the parents to pay early attention.
  - 母亲(親)感受到巳微弱的心跳伴随着温(隨著溫)柔的希望。
    - Mǔqīn gǎnshòudào sì wēiruò de xīntiào bànsuízhe wēnróu de xīwàng.
    - The mother felt the fetus's faint heartbeat accompanied by a gentle hope.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 飛
- **definition:** fly; flutter; hover; rush
- **pinyin:** fēi
- **components:**
  - 升
    - shēng
    - rise
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bird flying upwards, resembles a tasseled 升 (shēng, "rise")
  - **interpretation:** The character 飛(fēi, "fly") is a pictogram representing a bird in flight, capturing the upward motion and dynamic nature of flying. Its resemblance to 升 reflects the concept of rising or ascending, which is inherent to the action of flying.
  - **simplification:** The simplified form 飞(飛) was created by streamlining the strokes while maintaining the shape of the original pictogram.
- **examples:**
  - 小鸟(鳥)在蓝(藍)天中飛。
    - Xiǎo niǎo zài lántiān zhōng fēi.
    - The little bird flies in the blue sky.
  - 风筝(風箏)在空中飛，云(雲)朵悠然飛。
    - Fēngzhēng zài kōngzhōng fēi, yúnduǒ yōurán fēi.
    - The kite flies in the sky, and the clouds hover gracefully.
  - 燕子掠过(過)屋檐飛，春风(風)中悠然飛。
    - Yànzi luèguò wūyán fēi, chūnfēng zhōng yōurán fēi.
    - The swallow flies past the eaves, and in the spring breeze it soars gracefully.
### 起( )飞(飛) → 飛 → 升
- **definition:** rise
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a dipper ->
    - used to represent volume or measure
  - **interpretation:** The character 升(shēng, 'rise') originally depicted a measuring device, like a dipper, used for rice or liquids, emphasizing its function related to measurement or capacity.
- **examples:**
  - 太阳(陽)升起了。
    - Tàiyáng shēngqǐ le.
    - The sun has risen.
  - 太阳缓缓(陽緩緩)升起，照亮大地。
    - Tàiyáng huǎn huǎn shēngqǐ, zhàoliàng dàdì.
    - The sun slowly rises, illuminating the earth.

## 停( )车(車)场(場)
---
## parking lot
### tíngchēchǎng
---
- **traditional:** 停車場
- **definition:** parking lot
- **pinyin:** tíngchēchǎng
- **components:**
  - 停
    - tíng
    - stop; halt
  - 車
    - chē
    - vehicle; car
  - 場
    - chǎng
    - field; place; venue
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 停 (tíng, "stop"), 車 (chē, "vehicle"), 場 (chǎng, "field; place")
  - **interpretation:** The word 停車場 (tíngchēchǎng) combines 停 (tíng, "stop"), 車 (chē, "vehicle"), and 場 (chǎng, "field; place") to refer to a designated area where vehicles are stopped and parked. This combination makes sense because it specifies a place specifically meant for the cessation and storage of vehicles.
- **examples:**
  - 停车场(車場)很大。
    - Tíngchēchǎng hěn dà.
    - The parking lot is very large.
  - 我去停车场(車場)，寻(尋)找一个(個)空位。
    - Wǒ qù tíngchēchǎng, xúnzhǎo yīgè kòngwèi.
    - I go to the parking lot to look for an empty spot.
  - 早晨上班时(時)，停车场(車場)已经满(經滿)了。
    - Zǎochén shàngbān shí, tíngchēchǎng yǐjīng mǎnle.
    - During the morning rush, the parking lot is already full.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停
- **definition:** stop; halt
- **pinyin:** tíng
- **components:**
  - 亻
    - rén
    - person
  - 亭
    - tíng
    - pavilion
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Semantic 亻 (rén, "person") + Phonetic 亭 (tíng, "pavilion") ->
    - associated with a place where people stop or rest ->
    - "to stop; to park"
  - **interpretation:** The character 停(tíng) combines the person radical 亻 to show that stopping is an action related to humans, with the phonetic component 亭 to provide pronunciation. The meaning evolves from a person staying or pausing, similar to resting in a pavilion.
- **examples:**
  - 车(車)子停在路旁边(邊)。
    - Chēzǐ tíng zài lù pángbiān.
    - The car stopped by the roadside.
  - 司机(機)停车时(車時)，调(調)整方向后(後)再出发(發)。
    - Sījī tíngchē shí, tiáozhěng fāngxiàng hòu zài chūfā.
    - The driver, after parking, adjusted the steering before setting off again.
  - 因为(為)大雪，学(學)校停课(課)。
    - Yīnwèi dàxuě, xuéxiào tíngkè.
    - Due to heavy snow, school classes were canceled.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亻
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 亻 (rén, "person") is a stylization of 人 (rén, "person") ->
    - simplified for use as a component in other characters
  - **interpretation:** 亻 (rén, "person") is used as a component form of 人 (rén, "person") in compound characters, representing the human or person-related aspect.
- **examples:**
  - 亻是构(構)成许(許)多汉(漢)字的关键(關鍵)部首。
    - Rén shì gòuchéng xǔduō hànzì de guānjiàn bùshǒu.
    - The radical 亻 is a key component in many Chinese characters.
  - 学习汉(學習漢)字时(時)，了解亻的意义(義)很重要。
    - Xuéxí hànzì shí, liǎojiě rén de yìyì hěn zhòngyào.
    - When learning Chinese characters, understanding the meaning of 亻 is important.
  - 古人造字时(時)常取亻以表达(達)人物情感，因此亻贯(貫)穿于(於)文明史中。
    - Gǔrén zào zì shí cháng qǔ rén yǐ biǎodá rénwù qínggǎn, yīncǐ rén guànchuān yú wénmíng shǐ zhōng.
    - Ancient people often used the radical 亻 to express human emotions in character formation, and thus 亻 runs through the history of civilization.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亭
- **definition:** pavilion
- **pinyin:** tíng
- **components:**
  - 京
    - jīng
    - tower
  - 丁
    - dīng
    - nail
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 京 (jīng, "tower") + 丁 (dīng, "nail") =
    - tower form with phonetic nail ->
    - pavilion
  - **interpretation:** The character 亭 (tíng, "pavilion") combines the semantic 京 (jīng, "tower") representing the tall structure of a pavilion, with the phonetic 丁 (dīng, "nail") to indicate its pronunciation. This combination effectively conveys the concept of a constructed, stable, and prominent building used for leisure or shelter.
- **examples:**
  - 庭院里(裡)建有一座小亭。
    - Tíng yuàn lǐ jiàn yǒu yī zuò xiǎo tíng.
    - There is a small pavilion built in the courtyard.
  - 公园(園)中矗立一座亭，吸引众(眾)多游(遊)人。
    - Gōng yuán zhōng chù lì yī zuò tíng, xī yǐn zhòng duō yóu rén.
    - A pavilion stands tall in the park, attracting many visitors.
  - 湖边(邊)的小亭提供休息之所。
    - Hú biān de xiǎo tíng tí gōng xiū xí zhī suǒ.
    - The small pavilion by the lake provides a place to rest.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亭 → 京
- **definition:** tower
- **pinyin:** jīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tall structure resembling a tower
  - **interpretation:** The character 京(jīng, "tower") visually captures the essence of a tall, tower-like building. It is a straightforward representation using a simple, vertical form to suggest height.
- **examples:**
  - 山顶(頂)上矗立着(著)京，诉说着(訴說著)古老传说(傳說)。
    - Shāndǐng shàng chùlì zhe jīng, sùshuō zhe gǔlǎo chuánshuō.
    - The tower stands on the mountaintop, telling ancient legends.
  - 夜幕降临时(臨時)京闪烁着(閃爍著)光芒。
    - Yèmù jiànglín shí jīng shǎnshuò zhe guāngmáng.
    - At nightfall, the tower flickers with light.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 停 → 亭 → 丁
- **definition:** nail
- **pinyin:** dīng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts the head of a nail ->
    - 丁
  - **interpretation:** The character 丁 originally depicted the head of a nail, emphasizing simplicity and directness. While it has developed other interpretations over time, such as a head or city wall, these relate to similar shapes and functions. Today, 釘 (dīng, 'nail') reflects this meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 工人熟练(練)地把丁敲进(進)了墙(牆)壁。
    - Gōngrén shúliàn de bǎ dīng qiāng jìnle qiángbì.
    - The worker skillfully hammered the nail into the wall.
  - 他精心挑选(選)了铁质(鐵質)丁，确(確)保家具稳(傢俱穩)固。
    - Tā jīngxīn tiāoxuǎnle tiě zhì dīng, quèbǎo jiājù wěngù.
    - He carefully selected the iron nail to ensure the furniture was stable.
  - 请(請)把散落的丁收好。
    - Qǐng bǎ sànluò de dīng shōuhǎo.
    - Please gather the scattered nails.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 車
- **definition:** vehicle; car
- **pinyin:** chē
- **components:**
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a carriage viewed from above; wheels on both sides + sun shade on top ->
    - depicted vertically with wheels as strokes and loading area marked by 田 (tián, "field") ->
    - 車
  - **interpretation:** The character 車(chē, "vehicle") originally depicts a carriage from an overhead perspective. The transformation into the vertical form involved simplifying the depiction of wheels and emphasizing the loading area, marked by a field symbol, creating a streamlined pictographic representation.
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 車 was simplified to 车 by reducing the number of strokes, maintaining the overall shape of the vehicle but removing intricate details.
- **examples:**
  - 我坐车(車)去上班。
    - Wǒ zuò chē qù shàngbān.
    - I take a car to go to work.
  - 这辆车(這輛車)很快。
    - Zhè liàng chē hěn kuài.
    - This car is very fast.
  - 我想买(買)一辆(輛)新车(車)。
    - Wǒ xiǎng mǎi yī liàng xīn chē.
    - I want to buy a new car.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 車 → 田
- **definition:** field
- **pinyin:** tián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a field divided into four sections
  - **interpretation:** The character 田(tián, 'field') visually represents a field with sections, indicating its agricultural use and importance in ancient times.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民在田里(裡)耕作。
    - Nóngmín zài tián lǐ gēngzuò.
    - The farmer works in the field.
  - 那边(邊)的田长满(長滿)了庄(莊)稼，农(農)民收获(穫)忙碌。
    - Nàbiān de tián cháng mǎn le zhuāngjià, nóngmín shōuhuò mánglù.
    - The field over there is full of crops, and the farmer is busy harvesting.
  - 秋收时节(時節)，人们(們)忙于(於)收割田里(裡)的稻谷。
    - Qiūshōu shíjié, rénmen máng yú shōugē tián lǐ de dàogǔ.
    - During the harvest season, people are busy reaping the rice in the fields.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場
- **definition:** field; place; venue
- **pinyin:** chǎng
- **components:**
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
  - 昜
    - yáng
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 土 (tǔ, "earth") + phonetic 昜 (yáng) =
    - open field on the earth ->
    - field or place
  - **interpretation:** The character 場 combines the earth radical 土 (tǔ, "earth") with 昜 (yáng) to indicate a physical location or field. The semantic component 土 emphasizes the connection to the ground or land, while 昜 provides the phonetic aspect.
- **examples:**
  - 运动场(運動場)上人潮汹涌(洶湧)。
    - Yùn dòng chǎng shàng rén cháo xiōng yǒng.
    - Crowds surge on the sports field.
  - 这个场(這個場)地很宽(寬)敞，适(適)合举办(舉辦)大型演唱会(會)。
    - Zhè gè chǎng dì hěn kuān chǎng, shì hé jǔ bàn dà xíng yǎn chàng huì.
    - This venue is spacious and suitable for hosting large concerts.
  - 音乐会场(樂會場)中回荡着(蕩著)美妙旋律。
    - Yīn yuè huì chǎng zhōng huí dàng zhe měi miào xuán lǜ.
    - Beautiful melodies resonate in the concert hall.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜
- **pinyin:** yáng
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 丂
    - kǎo
    - breath
  - 彡
    - xiǎn
    - rays of light
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 日 (rì, "sun") + 丂 (kǎo, "breath") + 彡 (xiǎn, "rays of light") =
    - rays of the sun shining over a tree branch
  - **interpretation:** The character 昜(yáng) portrays the concept of the sun's rays shining down, symbolized by 日 (rì, "sun") with 丂 representing a tree branch and 彡 depicting the sun's rays. This compound visually encapsulates the light given off by the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 日光照耀下时(時)，旗帜(幟)高昜飘扬(飄揚)。
    - Rìguāng zhàoyào xià shí, qízhì gāo yáng piāoyáng.
    - Under the shining sunlight, the flag is raised high.
  - 风儿(風兒)吹过(過)柳梢时(時)，心中的梦(夢)想也随(隨)昜起。
    - Fēng ér chuīguò liǔ shāo shí, xīn zhōng de mèngxiǎng yě suí yáng qǐ.
    - As the wind passes the tips of the willows, the dreams in the heart rise as well.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜 → 日
- **definition:** sun
- **pinyin:** rì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the sun; a dot or line added in the center to distinguish from similar characters e.g. 囗
  - **interpretation:** As a pictogram, 日(rì, 'sun') directly represents the sun. In ancient times, the added dot helped visually differentiate it from other characters. This is analogous to the astronomical symbol ☉ and Egyptian hieroglyph 𓇳, both depicting the sun.
- **examples:**
  - 晨曦来临时(來臨時)，日出东(東)方。
    - Chénxī láilín shí, rìchū dōngfāng.
    - At the break of dawn, the sun rises in the east.
  - 温(溫)暖的日光洒满(灑滿)大地。
    - Wēnnuǎn de rìguāng sǎ mǎn dàdì.
    - The warm sunlight spreads over the earth.
  - 中午时(時)分，日高挂(掛)天。
    - Zhōngwǔ shífēn, rì gāo guà tiān.
    - At noon, the sun hangs high in the sky.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜 → 丂
- **definition:** breath
- **pinyin:** kǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts vapor rising from a source ->
    - original form for related phonetic characters
  - **interpretation:** The character 丂 originally depicted a breath or vapor rising, capturing the essence of something intangible or transient. It later became associated with various derivative forms indicating air or breath.
### 停( )车(車)场(場) → 場 → 昜 → 彡
- **definition:** rays of light
- **pinyin:** xiǎn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts three strands of hair ->
    - used to indicate three light rays in certain contexts
  - **interpretation:** 彡(shān, "rays") originally depicted strands of hair but also came to represent light rays, reflecting a change in symbolic meaning over time. Its use as a representation of 'ornament' and in characters like 昜 and 參 highlights its versatility in indicating rays or decorative elements.
- **examples:**
  - 天空洒(灑)下金色的彡，大地迎来温(來溫)暖。
    - Tiānkōng sǎ xià jīnsè de shān, dàdì yíng lái wēnnuǎn.
    - The sky showers golden rays, and the earth welcomes warmth.
  - 晨曦中的彡闪(閃)耀着(著)希望。
    - Chénxī zhōng de shān shǎnyào zhe xīwàng.
    - The rays in the morning light shine with hope.

## 停( )车(車)场(場)
### tíngchēchǎng
