## 菜( )单(單)
---
## menu
### càidān
---
- **traditional:** 菜單
- **definition:** menu
- **pinyin:** càidān
- **components:**
  - 菜
    - cài
    - vegetable; dish
  - 单(單)
    - dān
    - list
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 菜 (cài, "vegetable; dish") + 单(單) (dān, "list") =
    - 菜單(单) (càidān, "menu")
  - **interpretation:** The word 菜單(单) (càidān) combines 菜 (cài, "vegetable; dish") which refers to food or dishes, and 单(單) (dān, "list") indicating a list or record. Together, it logically refers to a list of dishes, or a menu. This reflects the exact purpose of a menu as it provides a list of dishes available to choose from.
- **examples:**
  - 请给(請給)我看菜单(單)，我想点(點)一道菜。
    - Qǐng gěi wǒ kàn càidān, wǒ xiǎng diǎn yī dào cài.
    - Please show me the menu, I want to order a dish.
  - 这里(這裡)的菜单(單)很丰(豐)富。
    - Zhèlǐ de càidān hěn fēngfù.
    - The menu here is very diverse.
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜
- **definition:** vegetable; dish
- **pinyin:** cài
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass; plant
  - 采
    - cǎi
    - pluck
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass; plant") + phonetic 采 (cǎi, "pluck") =
    - concept of plants gathered for consumption ->
    - vegetable; dish
  - **interpretation:** The character 菜(cài) conveys the idea of plants that are gathered, emphasizing the connection between agriculture and cuisine. The 艹 component implies vegetation, while 采 provides the phonetic cue and ties to the action of picking or collecting.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)道菜很美味。
    - Zhè dào cài hěn měiwèi.
    - This dish is very delicious.
  - 他擅长(長)烹饪(飪)，创(創)新菜式不断涌现(斷湧現)。
    - Tā shàncháng pēngrèn, chuàngxīn càishì bùduàn yǒngxiàn.
    - He excels at cooking, and innovative dishes keep emerging.
  - 街边(邊)小摊(攤)的菜色丰(豐)富。
    - Jiēbiān xiǎotān de càisè fēngfù.
    - The street vendor's variety of dishes is abundant.
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜 → 艹
- **definition:** grass; plant
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他写(寫)字时(時)用艹作草字的偏旁。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春天到来时(來時)，艹生长(長)得很快。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜 → 采(採)
- **traditional:** 採
- **definition:** pluck
- **pinyin:** cǎi
- **components:**
  - 爪
    - zhǎo
    - claw
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 爪 (zhǎo, 'claw') + 木 (mù, 'tree') =
    - hand grasping tree branch ->
    - pluck
  - **interpretation:** The character 采(cǎi, 'pluck') visually represents a claw or hand reaching out to a tree, symbolizing the action of plucking or gathering. This illustrates the intuitive meaning through its pictorial components.
  - **simplification:** In contemporary Chinese, 采(cǎi) serves both phonetic and semantic functions. The simplified form replaces the traditional form 採(cǎi), which is composed of 扌(shǒu, 'hand') + 采(cǎi, 'pluck'), illustrating the action of plucking with a hand.
- **examples:**
  - 她在花园里采(園裡採)花。
    - Tā zài huāyuán lǐ cǎi huā.
    - She is plucking flowers in the garden.
  - 我和朋友一同去山上采(採)果，享受自然。
    - Wǒ hé péngyǒu yītóng qù shān shàng cǎi guǒ, xiǎngshòu zìrán.
    - My friend and I go to pluck fruits on the mountain, enjoying nature.
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜 → 采(採) → 爪
- **definition:** claw
- **pinyin:** zhǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a hand grabbing from above, resembles a claw ->
    - stylized to represent claws
  - **interpretation:** The character 爪 (zhǎo, "claw") originally depicted a hand grabbing from above, stylized to resemble the form of claws.
- **examples:**
  - 猫(貓)的爪非常敏捷。
    - Māo de zhǎo fēicháng mǐnjié.
    - The cat's claws are very agile.
  - 狗的爪稳(穩)固，使它轻松(輕鬆)爬山。
    - Gǒu de zhǎo wěngù, shǐ tā qīngsōng páshān.
    - The dog's claws are sturdy, allowing it to climb mountains easily.
  - 鹰(鷹)的爪锋(鋒)利，能牢牢抓住猎(獵)物。
    - Yīng de zhǎo fēnglì, néng láoláo zhuā zhù lièwù.
    - The eagle's claws are sharp, enabling it to firmly grasp its prey.
### 菜( )单(單) → 菜 → 采(採) → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
### 菜( )单(單) → 单(單)
- **traditional:** 單
- **definition:** list
- **pinyin:** dān
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Unorthodox variant of 單.
  - **description:**
    - Pictogram of a Y-shaped wooden stick A + two stones attached on top B =
    - weapon for hunting ->
    - later stylized to resemble 口 (kǒu, 'mouth') resembling 中 (zhōng, 'middle') ->
    - further stylized as 田 (tián, 'field') with additional horizontal stroke below ->
    - final form 單.
  - **interpretation:** The character 單 intuitively represents a hunting tool or weapon, emphasizing its initial function and eventual simplification and stylization over time. The component 单 in this case represents a simplified form, which might have been used for practical writing needs.
  - **simplification:** 單 was simplified to 单 by eliminating additional strokes, creating a more straightforward representation that aligns with modern writing practices.
- **examples:**
  - 请将参(請將參)加聚会(會)的人员(員)名单准备(單準備)好。
    - Qǐng jiāng cānjiā jùhuì de rényuán míngdān zhǔnbèi hǎo.
    - Please prepare the list of people attending the party.
  - 老师检(師檢)查了学(學)生考试(試)名单(單)。
    - Lǎoshī jiǎnchá le xuéshēng kǎoshì míngdān.
    - The teacher checked the list of students taking the exam.
  - 经(經)理整理了客户订购单(戶訂購單)。
    - Jīnglǐ zhěnglǐ le kèhù dìnggòu dān.
    - The manager organized the customers' order list.
### 菜( )单(單) → 单(單) → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张开(張開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
### 菜( )单(單) → 单(單) → 田
- **definition:** field
- **pinyin:** tián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a field divided into four sections
  - **interpretation:** The character 田(tián, 'field') visually represents a field with sections, indicating its agricultural use and importance in ancient times.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民在田里(裡)耕作。
    - Nóngmín zài tián lǐ gēngzuò.
    - The farmer works in the field.
  - 那边(邊)的田长满(長滿)了庄(莊)稼，农(農)民收获(穫)忙碌。
    - Nàbiān de tián cháng mǎn le zhuāngjià, nóngmín shōuhuò mánglù.
    - The field over there is full of crops, and the farmer is busy harvesting.
  - 秋收时节(時節)，人们(們)忙于(於)收割田里(裡)的稻谷。
    - Qiūshōu shíjié, rénmen máng yú shōugē tián lǐ de dàogǔ.
    - During the harvest season, people are busy reaping the rice in the fields.

## menu

## 渴
---
## thirsty
### kě
---
- **definition:** thirsty
- **pinyin:** kě
- **components:**
  - 氵
    - shuǐ
    - water
  - 曷
    - hé
    - dry
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 氵(水) (shuǐ, "water") + phonetic: 曷 (hé, "dry") =
    - dry or exhausted of water ->
    - thirsty
  - **interpretation:** The character 渴(kě, "thirsty") combines the water radical 氵(水) to indicate the relation to water, with 曷 (hé, "dry") as the phonetic component, suggesting dryness or a lack of water, which directly conveys the concept of thirst.
- **examples:**
  - 我感觉(覺)非常渴。
    - Wǒ gǎnjué fēicháng kě.
    - I feel very thirsty.
  - 长时间运动后(長時間運動後)，他开(開)始感到渴。
    - Cháng shíjiān yùndòng hòu, tā kāishǐ gǎndào kě.
    - After long exercise, he started to feel thirsty.
  - 口渴时(時)，喝一杯冰水很解乏。
    - Kǒu kě shí, hē yì bēi bīngshuǐ hěn jiěfá.
    - When thirsty, drinking a glass of iced water is very refreshing.
### 渴 → 氵
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 氵is the radical form of 水 (shuǐ, "water") ->
    - depicts flowing water, compressed and stylized next to characters.
  - **interpretation:** The character 氵is a simplified variant used as a radical to represent water-related meanings in other characters. It retains the flowing water depiction of 水 (shuǐ, "water") but is stylized to fit alongside other components.
- **examples:**
  - 水是生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 汉(漢)字中偏旁氵，代表水。
    - Hànzì zhōng piān páng shuǐ, dàibiǎo shuǐ.
    - In Chinese characters, the radical '氵' signifies water.
  - 河水清澈透明，鱼儿欢(魚兒歡)快戏(戲)水。
    - Hé shuǐ qīngchè tòumíng, yú er huānkuaì xì shuǐ.
    - The river water is clear and transparent, and the fish happily play in it.
### 渴 → 曷
- **definition:** dry
- **pinyin:** hé
- **components:**
  - 匃
    - gài
    - lack
  - 曰
    - yuē
    - say
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - phonetic 匃 (gài, "lack") + semantic 曰 (yuē, "say") ->
    - final form 曷
  - **interpretation:** The character 曷(hé, "dry") combines 匃 (gài, "lack") as a phonetic component and 曰 (yuē, "say") as the semantic component. The depiction could suggest a lack or absence, which by extension relates to the meaning "dry" as it implies the absence of moisture.
### 渴 → 曷 → 匃
- **definition:** lack
- **pinyin:** gài
- **components:**
  - 丐
    - gài
    - beggar; lack
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant character
  - **description:** 匃 is a variant form of 丐 (gài, "beggar; lack")
  - **interpretation:** The character 匃 is a variant form of 丐 (gài, "beggar; lack"), sharing a similar meaning and usage in the context of indicating lack or poverty. It is not frequently used in modern writing, where 丐 is the standard form.
### 渴 → 曷 → 匃 → 丐
- **definition:** beggar; lack
- **pinyin:** gài
- **components:**
  - 匄
    - gài
    - original meaning unknown
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Corruption of 匄 (gài, original meaning unknown) ->
    - final form 丐 (gài, 'beggar')
  - **interpretation:** 丐 (gài) is derived from 匄, which originally had an unknown meaning, possibly 'to damage'. Over time, 丐 evolved into its current use to mean 'beggar'. The transformation appears to involve a simplification or corruption of the original form, indicating a shift in both form and meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 街上有个(個)丐，他四处讨饭(處討飯)。
    - Jiē shàng yǒu gè gài, tā sì chù tǎo fàn.
    - There is a beggar on the street, and he begs for food everywhere.
  - 他曾是繁华(華)都市边缘(邊緣)的丐，今日落魄街头(頭)。
    - Tā céng shì fán huá dū shì biān yuán de gài, jīn rì luò pò jiē tóu.
    - He used to be a beggar on the outskirts of a bustling city, but today he is destitute on the street.
### 渴 → 曷 → 匃 → 丐 → 匄
- **definition:** original meaning unknown
- **pinyin:** gài
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
  - 亡
    - wáng
    - tip
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") with a component resembling the tip of a blade 亡
  - **interpretation:** The character 匄(gài) originally depicted a knife 刀 (dāo, "knife") with a tip or component resembling the tip of a blade 亡. The original meaning is thought to be related to 'damage', though it is not fully clear.
### 渴 → 曷 → 匃 → 丐 → 匄 → 刀
- **definition:** knife
- **pinyin:** dāo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a knife
  - **interpretation:** 刀 (dāo, "knife") is a pictographic representation of a knife or blade, with a sharp edge and a handle, resembling the form of a basic cutting tool.
- **examples:**
  - 他用锋(鋒)利的刀，切开(開)蔬菜。
    - tā yòng fēnglì de dāo, qiē kāi shūcài.
    - He uses a sharp knife to cut vegetables.
  - 这(這)把刀非常锋(鋒)利。
    - zhè bǎ dāo fēicháng fēnglì.
    - This knife is very sharp.
  - 厨师(廚師)小心地持刀，为(為)客人切肉。
    - chúshī xiǎoxīn de chí dāo, wèi kèrén qiē ròu.
    - The chef holds the knife carefully and slices meat for the guest.
### 渴 → 曷 → 匃 → 丐 → 匄 → 亡
- **definition:** tip
- **pinyin:** wáng
- **components:**
  - 刀
    - dāo
    - knife
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on 刀 (dāo, "knife") indicates cutting edge ->
    - disappearance of knowledge ->
    - perish
  - **interpretation:** The character 亡(wáng) visually represents the sharp, cutting edge of a knife, which metaphorically implies the loss of life or things 'perishing'. Over time, it came to signify broader concepts of disappearance and extinction.
- **examples:**
  - 国(國)破，家亡。
    - Guó pò, jiā wáng.
    - The country is broken, the family perishes.
  - 经过(經過)激战时(戰時)，士兵亡。
    - Jīngguò jīzhàn shí, shìbīng wáng.
    - During the intense battle, the soldiers perished.
### 渴 → 曷 → 曰
- **definition:** say
- **pinyin:** yuē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth, signifying speech
  - **interpretation:** The character 曰 (yuē, "say") visually resembles a mouth or an opening, symbolizing the action of speaking or saying something.
- **examples:**
  - 老师(師)曰：勤奋(奮)是成功之母。
    - Lǎoshī yuē：qínfèn shì chénggōng zhī mǔ。
    - The teacher said, 'Diligence is the mother of success.'
  - 孔子曰，学(學)而不思则(則)罔。
    - Kǒngzǐ yuē, xué ér bù sī zé wǎng。
    - Confucius said, 'Learning without thought leads to confusion.'
  - 老子曰，无为(無為)而治。
    - Lǎozǐ yuē, wúwéi ér zhì。
    - Laozi said, 'Governance should be achieved through non-action.'

## 熊
---
## bear
### xióng
---
- **definition:** bear
- **pinyin:** xióng
- **components:**
  - 能
    - néng
    - bear
  - 炎
    - yán
    - flame
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 能 (néng, "bear") + stylized form of 炎 (yán, "flame") =
    - original onomatopoeic word for "raging flame" ->
    - borrowed to mean "bear"
  - **interpretation:** The character 熊(xióng) was initially an onomatopoeic term for the raging flame, where the semantic element, 能 (néng, "bear"), indicates its original meaning. It was later borrowed to signify "bear" when the concept required a representation, utilizing the abbreviated form of 炎 (yán, "flame") as the phonetic component.
- **examples:**
  - 那只(隻)熊看起来(來)很可爱(愛)。
    - Nà zhī xióng kàn qǐlái hěn kě'ài.
    - That bear looks very cute.
  - 森林里(裡)有很多熊，人们(們)也要小心。
    - Sēnlín lǐ yǒu hěn duō xióng, rénmen yě yào xiǎoxīn.
    - There are many bears in the forest, and people must be careful.
  - 冬天来临时(來臨時)，熊会准备过(會準備過)冬。
    - Dōngtiān láilín shí, xióng huì zhǔnbèi guòdōng.
    - When winter comes, bears prepare for winter.
### 熊 → 能
- **definition:** bear
- **pinyin:** néng
- **components:**
  - 匕
    - bǐ
    - spoon
  - 月
    - yuè
    - moon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bear: two paws stylized as 匕 (bǐ, "spoon") + face/mouth stylized as 月 (yuè, "moon")
  - **interpretation:** The character 能(néng), originally meant to represent a bear, combines elements stylized as paws and a face to visually convey an animal's features. Over time, this depiction of a bear has lent its phonetic value to words associated with ability and energy.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)座桥(橋)能承受大风(風)。
    - Zhè zuò qiáo néng chéngshòu dà fēng.
    - This bridge can bear strong winds.
  - 他能承受巨大压(壓)力。
    - Tā néng chéngshòu jùdà yālì.
    - He can bear tremendous pressure.
  - 这(這)台电脑(電腦)能运(運)行复杂(複雜)程序，满(滿)足现(現)代需求。
    - Zhè tái diànnǎo néng yùnxíng fùzá chéngxù, mǎnzú xiàndài xūqiú.
    - This computer can run complex programs, meeting modern needs.
### 熊 → 能 → 匕
- **definition:** spoon
- **pinyin:** bǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the shape of a spoon or dagger, indicating an object with a handle.
  - **interpretation:** The character 匕 (bǐ, "cane") originally depicts a spoon or dagger, highlighting its application as a tool with a handle, which conceptually relates to a cane.
- **examples:**
  - 他用匕支撑(撐)自己，慢慢走过(過)崎岖(嶇)的小路。
    - Tā yòng bǐ zhīchēng zìjǐ, màn màn zǒuguò qíqū de xiǎolù.
    - He supports himself with his cane, and slowly walks along the rugged path.
  - 老人依靠匕，缓缓(緩緩)行走在乡间(鄉間)小道。
    - Lǎorén yīkào bǐ, huǎn huǎn xíngzǒu zài xiāngjiān xiǎodào.
    - The old man relies on his cane, and gently walks on the country lane.
### 熊 → 能 → 月
- **definition:** moon
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a crescent moon
  - **interpretation:** The character 月(yuè, "moon") is a pictographic representation of a crescent moon, straightforwardly capturing the curved shape often associated with the moon's appearance. Though interchangeable with 夕 (xī, "evening") in the past, it distinctly represents the moon in this usage.
- **examples:**
  - 夜空挂着(掛著)明月。
    - Yè kōng guà zhe míng yuè.
    - The bright moon hangs in the night sky.
  - 人们赏(們賞)月，寄托(託)相思。
    - Rén men shǎng yuè, jì tuō xiāng sī.
    - People enjoy the moon, expressing their longing.
### 熊 → 炎
- **definition:** flame
- **pinyin:** yán
- **components:**
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 火 (huǒ, 'fire') + 火 (huǒ, 'fire') =
    - two fires together ->
    - flame, inflammation
  - **interpretation:** The character combines two 火 (huǒ, 'fire') symbols, emphasizing an intense or extensive fire. This conveys the meanings of 'flame' and 'inflammation', as both involve a spreading or intensified heat.
- **examples:**
  - 他因感冒导(導)致喉咙(嚨)炎。
    - Tā yīn gǎnmào dǎozhì hóulóng yán.
    - He developed throat inflammation due to a cold.
  - 壁炉里(爐裡)燃烧着(燒著)炎。
    - Bìlú lǐ ránshāo zhe yán.
    - Flames are burning in the fireplace.
### 熊 → 炎 → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火在壁炉(爐)中熊熊燃烧(燒)。
    - Huǒ zài bìlú zhōng xióngxióng ránshāo.
    - The fire burns fiercely in the fireplace.
  - 野外露营时(營時)，火能驱(驅)走寒冷。
    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇到火灾时(災時)，迅速疏散最为(為)重要。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.

## 害怕
---
## to be afraid
### hàipà
---
- **definition:** to be afraid
- **pinyin:** hàipà
- **components:**
  - 害
    - hài
    - harm; injure; evil; calamity
  - 怕
    - pà
    - fear; dread; afraid
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 害 (hài, "harm") + 怕 (pà, "fear") means to experience fear or be afraid of something bad happening.
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 害 (hài, "harm") and 怕 (pà, "fear") suggests the feeling of fear that arises from the anticipation of potential harm or danger.
- **examples:**
  - 我害怕大雨。
    - Wǒ hàipà dàyǔ.
    - I am afraid of heavy rain.
  - 当(當)夜深人静时(靜時)，我害怕孤独(獨)。
    - Dāng yè shēn rén jìng shí, wǒ hàipà gūdú.
    - When the night is quiet, I am afraid of loneliness.
### 害怕 → 害
- **definition:** harm; injure; evil; calamity
- **pinyin:** hài
- **components:**
  - 宀
    - mián
    - roof
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 丯
    - jiè
    - aid
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Semantic 宀 (mián, "roof") + Semantic 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + Phonetic 丯 =
    - a structure covering a vocal element, suggesting confinement or restriction ->
    - harm
  - **interpretation:** The character 害(hài) consists of a roof 宀, representing a covered or enclosed space, combined with 口, indicating concepts related to speech or mouth. The phonetic 丯 helps to articulate the sound. Together, the character conveys the idea of harm as being restricted or constrained, perhaps metaphorically linked to being silenced or confined under the roof.
- **examples:**
  - 虚(虛)假的信息会(會)害人。
    - xūjiǎ de xìnxī huì hài rén.
    - False information harms people.
  - 谣(謠)言散播，必然会(會)害到社会(會)。
    - yáoyán sànbō, bìrán huì hài dào shèhuì.
    - Spreading rumors will certainly harm society.
  - 一时(時)的愤(憤)怒会(會)害自己，招来(來)麻烦(煩)。
    - yīshí de fènnù huì hài zìjǐ, zhāo lái máfan.
    - A moment of anger will harm oneself and invite trouble.
### 害怕 → 害 → 宀
- **definition:** roof
- **pinyin:** mián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a house with four walls ->
    - roof
  - **interpretation:** 宀(mián, "roof") is a pictogram representing a house with four walls. It emphasizes an enclosed space, distinguishing it from similar structures like 广(guǎng, "broad") which depicts a building with three walls. This makes 宀 a logical choice for representing a roof in various characters.
- **examples:**
  - 含有宀的汉(漢)字代表家的温(溫)暖。
    - Hán yǒu mián de hànzì dàibiǎo jiā de wēnnuǎn.
    - Chinese characters that include the radical '宀' represent the warmth of home.
  - 屋顶(頂)遮风挡(風擋)雨，家园(園)散发温(發溫)馨。
    - Wūdǐng zhē fēng dǎng yǔ, jiāyuán sànfā wēnxīn.
    - The roof shields from wind and rain, and the home radiates warmth.
### 害怕 → 害 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张开(張開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
### 害怕 → 害 → 丯
- **definition:** aid
- **pinyin:** jiè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts something carved/engraved ->
    - proto-form of 㓞 ->
    - variant of 王(玉)
  - **interpretation:** The character 丯 originally depicted something that was carved or engraved, serving as a proto-form of 㓞, which means 'cut'. It was later used as a variant of 玉 (yù, 'jade'), distinguished by adding 王 (wáng, 'king') to symbolize a king's authority.
### 害怕 → 怕
- **definition:** fear; dread; afraid
- **pinyin:** pà
- **components:**
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
  - 白
    - bái
    - white
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 心 (xīn, 'heart') + 白 (bái, 'white') =
    - heart combined with phonetic indicating sound ->
    - denotes fear or dread
  - **interpretation:** The character 怕(pà, 'fear; dread') combines the heart radical 心 (xīn, 'heart'), symbolizing emotions, with 白 (bái, 'white') for phonetic representation. The heart component reflects the emotional experience of fear, while the phonetic component guides its pronunciation.
- **examples:**
  - 我怕黑。
    - Wǒ pà hēi.
    - I am afraid of the dark.
  - 他怕狗，不敢靠近它。
    - Tā pà gǒu, bù gǎn kào jìn tā.
    - He is afraid of dogs, and does not dare to approach them.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stylized representation of a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, 'heart') visually represents the shape of a heart, emphasizing its central and essential role in both a physical and metaphorical sense.
- **examples:**
  - 他的心温(溫)暖无(無)比。
    - Tā de xīn wēnnuǎn wúbǐ.
    - His heart is incredibly warm.
  - 她把心放在艺术(藝術)上，追求完美。
    - Tā bǎ xīn fàng zài yìshù shàng, zhuīqiú wánměi.
    - She dedicates her heart to art, pursuing perfection.
  - 音乐(樂)直击(擊)心灵(靈)。
    - Yīnyuè zhí jī xīnlíng.
    - Music strikes straight at the heart (soul).
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白
- **definition:** white
- **pinyin:** bái
- **components:**
  - 樂(乐)
    - yuè
    - oak
  - 皂
    - zào
    - acorn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an acorn ->
    - used in 樂/乐 (oak) and 皂 (acorn) ->
    - meaning “white” derived from acorn's inside color
  - **interpretation:** The character 白(bái, "white") might originally depict an acorn, reflecting its usage in words related to oak and acorn, and the meaning of 'white' comes from the color of an acorn's interior. This interpretation connects the form with its current meaning of 'white.'
- **examples:**
  - 村后那处被称作‘白’的泉口(村後那處被稱作‘白’的泉口)，源源不断(斷)流出甘甜的泉水。
    - Cūn hòu nà chù bèi chēng zuò ‘Bái’ de quán kǒu, yuán yuán bù duàn liú chū gān tián de quán shuǐ.
    - The spring mouth behind the village, known as ‘Bái’, continuously gushes out sweet water.
  - 古镇传说(鎮傳說)，每逢春日便有白现(現)身，润泽(潤澤)山村。
    - Gǔ zhèn chuán shuō, měi féng chūn rì biàn yǒu Bái xiàn shēn, rùn zé shān cūn.
    - According to the legend of the ancient town, every spring a ‘Bái’ appears, nourishing the mountain village.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白 → 樂
- **definition:** oak
- **pinyin:** yuè
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - mì
    - string
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 白
    - bái
    - white
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 糸 (mì, "string") + 木 (mù, "wood") =
    - strings on a piece of wood ->
    - wooden musical instrument
  - **interpretation:** The character 樂 (lè, "music") originally represents strings attached to a wooden frame, depicting a musical instrument. The addition of 白 (bái) in bronze inscriptions likely represents either the thumb in playing motion or serves as a phonetic component. Over time, it became associated with music and by extension, happiness.
- **examples:**
  - 我喜歡聽樂。
    - Wǒ xǐhuān tīng lè.
    - I like listening to music.
  - 他在音樂會上欣賞樂，感受文化魅力。
    - Tā zài yīnyuèhuì shàng xīnshǎng lè, gǎnshòu wénhuà mèilì.
    - He appreciates music at the concert and experiences the charm of culture.
  - 書房中傳來樂，令人心情愉悅。
    - Shūfáng zhōng chuán lái lè, lìngrén xīnqíng yúyuè.
    - Music comes from the study, making people feel delighted.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白 → 樂 → 糸
- **definition:** string
- **pinyin:** mì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这个设计图(這個設計圖)必须(須)用细(細)糸画(畫)出来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我们参观(們參觀)了古代的织(織)布技术(術)，对丝绸制(對絲綢製)作产(產)生了兴(興)趣。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白 → 樂 → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白 → 皂
- **definition:** acorn
- **pinyin:** zào
- **components:**
  - 皁
    - zào
    - acorn
  - 早
    - zǎo
    - early
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form
  - **description:** 皂 (zào) is a variant form of 皁, which is in turn a variant form of 早 (zǎo, "early") retaining its original sense "acorn."
  - **interpretation:** 皂 (zào) originally represented the concept of "acorn" before it was adapted to signify colors such as black. This transformation shows the fluidity of meanings as characters evolved over time.
- **examples:**
  - 秋风(風)吹过树(過樹)林时(時)，地上落满(滿)了皂和落叶(葉)。
    - qiū fēng chuīguò shùlín shí, dìshàng luò mǎn le zào hé luòyè.
    - When the autumn wind blows through the forest, the ground is covered with acorns and fallen leaves.
  - 山野中不时(時)有皂掉落，象征着(徵著)秋天的丰(豐)收。
    - shānyě zhōng bùshí yǒu zào diàoluò, xiàngzhēng zhe qiūtiān de fēngshōu.
    - In the hills and fields, acorns occasionally fall, symbolizing the abundant harvest of autumn.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白 → 皂 → 皁
- **definition:** acorn
- **pinyin:** zào
- **components:**
  - 皂
    - zào
    - acorn
  - 早
    - zǎo
    - early
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant
  - **description:** 皁 (zào, 'acorn') is a variant traditional form of 皂 (zào) which retains the original sense of 'acorn'. It is also a variant form of 早 (zǎo, 'early'), symbolizing the early development or sprouting of an acorn in nature.
  - **interpretation:** 皁 (zào) illustrates how certain characters retain historical meanings through variant forms while connecting to their roots, in this case, through semantic borrowing from 早 (zǎo, 'early') relating to acorns as an early stage of development.
### 害怕 → 怕 → 白 → 皂 → 皁 → 早
- **definition:** early
- **pinyin:** zǎo
- **components:**
  - 日
    - rì
    - sun
  - 甲
    - jiǎ
    - first
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - Early pictogram depicts an acorn ->
    - borrowed phonetically for 'morning' ->
    - Late bronze inscriptions: semantic 日 (rì, 'sun') + phonetic 棗(枣) (zǎo) ->
    - small seal script: 日(日, 'sun') + 甲(甲, 'first') =
    - when the sun first rises ->
    - 'early'
  - **interpretation:** The character evolved from depicting an acorn to incorporating the image of the sun and the concept of 'first,' symbolizing the sun's rise to indicate 'early.' It's a combination of both semantic elements and phonetic borrowing.
- **examples:**
  - 我今天起床很早。
    - Wǒ jīntiān qǐchuáng hěn zǎo.
    - I woke up very early today.
  - 他早到办(辦)公室，开(開)始了紧张(緊張)的会议(會議)。
    - Tā zǎo dào bàngōngshì, kāishǐ le jǐnzhāng de huìyì.
    - He arrived at the office early and started a busy meeting.
  - 他喜欢(歡)早睡，早起的习惯让(習慣讓)他精力充沛。
    - Tā xǐhuān zǎo shuì, zǎo qǐ de xíguàn ràng tā jīnglì chōngpèi.
    - He likes going to bed early, and his habit of getting up early makes him energetic.

## 棵
---
## measure word for trees and plants
### kē
---
- **definition:** measure word for trees and plants
- **pinyin:** kē
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
  - 柯
    - kē
    - none
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form
  - **description:**
    - 棵 is a variant form of 樖. 樖: 木 (mù, "wood") + 柯 (kē) =
    - measure word for trees, derived from structure and sound
  - **interpretation:** The character 棵 utilizes 木 (mù, "wood") combined with the phonetic 柯 (kē) to indicate its association with trees and plants. Being a variant form, it retains the meaning related to trees due to the presence of 木, playing off the phonetic element to denote its function as a measure word.
- **examples:**
  - 花园里(園裡)有一棵樱(櫻)花树(樹)。
    - Huāyuán lǐ yǒu yī kē yīnghuā shù。
    - There is a cherry tree in the garden.
  - 学(學)校门(門)前种(種)了两(兩)棵榕树(樹)，每当(當)微风(風)吹过(過)。
    - Xuéxiào mén qián zhǒngle liǎng kē róngshù, měi dāng wēifēng chuīguò。
    - Two banyan trees were planted in front of the school, and the gentle breeze passes by.
  - 山坡上长着(長著)一棵野生橡树(樹)，秋天时树叶变(時樹葉變)得金黄(黃)。
    - Shānpō shàng zhǎngzhe yī kē yěshēng xiàngshù, qiūtiān shí shùyè biàn dé jīnhuáng。
    - A wild oak grows on the hillside, and in autumn its leaves turn golden.
### 棵 → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
### 棵 → 柯
- **definition:** none
- **pinyin:** kē
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 可
    - kě
    - can
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 木 (mù, "tree") + phonetic: 可 (kě, "can") =
    - tree-related object ->
    - branch; axe handle
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 木 (mù, "tree"), signifying a wooden object, with 可 (kě, "can"), which provides the pronunciation. This reflects its meaning related to parts of a tree, such as branches or axe handles.
- **examples:**
  - 古斧的柯经过(經過)匠人的精心打磨，仍然结实(結實)。
    - Gǔ fǔ de kē jīngguò jiàngrén de jīngxīn dǎmó, réngrán jiéshí.
    - The axe handle of the ancient axe remains sturdy after the craftsman's meticulous polishing.
  - 老树(樹)的柯，承载着岁(載著歲)月的痕迹(跡)。
    - Lǎo shù de kē, chéngzài zhe suìyuè de hénjì.
    - The branch of the old tree bears the marks of time.
  - 他拿起斧头(頭)，细(細)看那光滑的柯。
    - Tā ná qǐ fǔtóu, xìkàn nà guānghuá de kē.
    - He picked up the axe and closely examined its smooth handle.
### 棵 → 柯 → 可
- **definition:** can
- **pinyin:** kě
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 丂
    - kǎo
    - exhaled air
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + phonetic: 丂 (kǎo) =
    - reference to exhaled air "to sing" ->
    - capability to perform actions
  - **interpretation:** This character combines the semantic element 口 (kǒu, "mouth") with the phonetic 丂 (kǎo), referencing exhaling or vocal actions like singing, which suggests expressing capability or permission.
- **examples:**
  - 你可尝试(嘗試)一下新方法。
    - Nǐ kě chángshì yīxià xīn fāngfǎ.
    - You may try a new method.
  - 此事虽难(雖難)，你可坚(堅)持到底。
    - Cǐ shì suī nán, nǐ kě jiānchí dàodǐ.
    - Although this matter is difficult, you may persist to the end.
### 棵 → 柯 → 可 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张开(張開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
### 棵 → 柯 → 可 → 丂
- **definition:** exhaled air
- **pinyin:** kǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts exhaled air coming from an open mouth
  - **interpretation:** The character 丂 (kǎo, "exhaled air") visually represents the movement or presence of air as it exits the mouth. The open shape suggests the flow or emission of breath.
---
## 棵
### kē

## 累(纍)
---
## tired
### lèi
---
- **traditional:** 纍
- **definition:** tired
- **pinyin:** lèi
- **components:**
  - 糸
    - sī
    - silk
  - 田
    - tián
    - field
  - 衣
    - yī
    - clothing
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form
  - **description:**
    - 糸 (sī, "silk") + 田 (tián, "field") + 衣 (yī, "clothing") =
    - layers of tied-up silk over fields and clothing ->
    - connected to repetition or tiring work ->
    - took on meaning of tired as 累
  - **interpretation:** The traditional character 纍 combines 糸 (sī, "silk") with 田 (tián, "field") and 衣 (yī, "clothing"), symbolizing repetitive, tiring work across fields using silk thread, ultimately leading to the sense of 'tired.' The current form 累 evolved as a simplified and variant traditional character maintaining this association.
  - **simplification:** 累 is a simplified version and variant form of 纍, which emphasizes ease of writing by reducing multiple repeated components.
- **examples:**
  - 我累了。
    - Wǒ lèi le.
    - I am tired.
  - 我工作了一整天，感到累。
    - Wǒ gōngzuò le yī zhěng tiān, gǎndào lèi.
    - I worked all day and feel tired.
  - 经过长时间(經過長時間)的学习(學習)，我感到累。
    - Jīngguò cháng shíjiān de xuéxí, wǒ gǎndào lèi.
    - After studying for a long time, I feel tired.
### 累(纍) → 糸
- **definition:** silk
- **pinyin:** sī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这个设计图(這個設計圖)必须(須)用细(細)糸画(畫)出来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我们参观(們參觀)了古代的织(織)布技术(術)，对丝绸制(對絲綢製)作产(產)生了兴(興)趣。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
### 累(纍) → 田
- **definition:** field
- **pinyin:** tián
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a field divided into four sections
  - **interpretation:** The character 田(tián, 'field') visually represents a field with sections, indicating its agricultural use and importance in ancient times.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民在田里(裡)耕作。
    - Nóngmín zài tián lǐ gēngzuò.
    - The farmer works in the field.
  - 那边(邊)的田长满(長滿)了庄(莊)稼，农(農)民收获(穫)忙碌。
    - Nàbiān de tián cháng mǎn le zhuāngjià, nóngmín shōuhuò mánglù.
    - The field over there is full of crops, and the farmer is busy harvesting.
  - 秋收时节(時節)，人们(們)忙于(於)收割田里(裡)的稻谷。
    - Qiūshōu shíjié, rénmen máng yú shōugē tián lǐ de dàogǔ.
    - During the harvest season, people are busy reaping the rice in the fields.
### 累(纍) → 衣
- **definition:** clothing
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a basic outline of a garment with sleeves hanging down.
  - **interpretation:** The character 衣 (yī, 'clothes') clearly resembles a simple garment, with parts representing sleeves and the body of clothing. This visual representation aligns with its meaning of 'clothes' or 'clothing.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)件衣很特别(別)。
    - Zhè jiàn yī hěn tè bié.
    - This piece of clothing is very special.
  - 冬天来(來)了，人们换(們換)上了暖和的衣。
    - Dōngtiān lái le, rénmen huàn shàng le nuǎn huó de yī.
    - Winter has arrived, and people put on warm clothes.
---
## 累(纍)
### lèi
---
## tired

## 树(樹)
---
## tree
### shù
---
- **traditional:** 樹
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** shù
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 尌
    - shù
    - phonetic component
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - semantic: 木 (mù, "tree") + phonetic: 尌 (shù) =
    - tree-like object described by 尌 ->
    - tree
  - **interpretation:** The character 树(樹) (shù, "tree") combines 木 (mù, "tree") for its meaning, and 尌 (shù) provides the pronunciation. Together, these components create a character that is pronounced like 尌 and relates to trees.
  - **simplification:** 树(樹): The simplified form retains 木 ("tree") while modifying 尌 to simplify strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 那棵树(樹)非常茂盛。
    - Nà kē shù fēicháng màoshèng.
    - That tree is very lush.
  - 微风(風)拂过树(過樹)梢，阳(陽)光洒满(灑滿)枝头(頭)。
    - Wēifēng fúguò shùshāo, yángguāng sǎ mǎn zhītóu.
    - A gentle breeze brushes the treetops, while sunlight fills the branches.
### 树(樹) → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
### 树(樹) → 尌
- **definition:** phonetic component
- **pinyin:** shù
- **components:**
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - hand
  - 豆
    - dòu
    - bean
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 木(樹) (mù, "tree") + 寸 (cùn, "hand") ->
    - symbolizing planting a tree originally ->
    - 豆 (dòu, "bean") added later as phonetic ->
    - 木 and 豆 fused into 壴 structure in modern form
  - **interpretation:** The character 尌 (shù) represents the act of planting a tree, depicted by combining a hand and a tree. Over time, 豆 (dòu, "bean") was added as a phonetic component, but in the contemporary version, components have become visually integrated into a single structure.
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 寸
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这块(這塊)布每一寸都是精心制(製)作。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用卷尺量一寸，每一寸数据(數據)都准确(準確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 豆
- **definition:** bean
- **pinyin:** dòu
- **components:**
  - 菽
    - shū
    - pulse
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a container ->
    - borrowed phonetically for the plant name
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicted a container, 豆 (dòu, 'drum') was phonetically borrowed to represent the plant name for beans, eventually displacing the term 菽 (shū, 'pulse'). It is unrelated to the 豊 (fēng, 'abundant') character.
- **examples:**
  - 祭司敲豆奏乐(樂)，引来(來)神灵(靈)祝福。
    - Jìsī qiāo dòu zòuyuè, yǐn lái shénlíng zhùfú.
    - The priest beats the drum, summoning divine blessings.
  - 古风庆(風慶)典上敲响(響)豆，唤(喚)起怀(懷)古情怀(懷)。
    - Gǔfēng qìngdiǎn shàng qiāoxiǎng dòu, huànqǐ huáigǔ qínghuái.
    - At the ancient-style celebration, the beating of the drum evokes nostalgic sentiments.
  - 豆声(聲)震天。
    - Dòu shēng zhèntiān.
    - The sound of the drum shakes the heavens.
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 豆 → 菽
- **definition:** pulse
- **pinyin:** shū
- **components:**
  - 艹
    - cǎo
    - grass
  - 叔
    - shū
    - uncle
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 艹 (cǎo, "grass") + 叔 (shū, "uncle") =
    - plant-related term with phonetic value from 叔
  - **interpretation:** The character 菽(shū, "pulse") combines the semantic 艹 (cǎo, "grass") to indicate a plant-related concept, with the phonetic element 叔 (shū) to suggest its pronunciation. This reflects the agricultural context of 'pulse' as a type of leguminous plant.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)人耕种(種)菽田，迎接秋收。
    - Nóng rén gēngzhòng shū tián, yíngjiē qiūshōu.
    - The farmers cultivate pulse fields, welcoming the autumn harvest.
  - 他用菽研磨出浓(濃)香豆浆(漿)，享受健康生活。
    - Tā yòng shū yánmó chū nóngxiāng dòujiāng, xiǎngshòu jiànkāng shēnghuó.
    - He grinds pulses to make fragrant soy milk, enjoying a healthy life.
  - 春天里(裏)菽花绽(綻)放。
    - Chūntiān lǐ shū huā zhànfàng.
    - In spring, the pulse flowers bloom.
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 豆 → 菽 → 艹
- **definition:** grass
- **pinyin:** cǎo
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts blades of grass
  - **interpretation:** 艹 is a pictogram representing grass or plants, resembling blades of grass. It is commonly used as a radical in other characters related to grass or vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 他写(寫)字时(時)用艹作草字的偏旁。
    - Tā xiězì shí yòng cǎo zuò cǎozì de piānpáng.
    - He uses '艹' as the radical for grass in his characters.
  - 春天到来时(來時)，艹生长(長)得很快。
    - Chūntiān dàolái shí, cǎo shēngzhǎng de hěn kuài.
    - When spring arrives, grass grows rapidly.
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 豆 → 菽 → 叔
- **definition:** uncle
- **pinyin:** shū
- **components:**
  - 尗
    - shū
    - wooden stake
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound and phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic 尗 (shū, "wooden stake") + semantic 又 (yòu, "hand") =
    - using a wooden stake to dig the ground ->
    - phonetically borrowed for "paternal uncle"
  - **interpretation:** The character 叔(shū, "uncle") originally depicted using a hand to plant a wooden stake, representing construction or foundation setting. This was later phonetically borrowed to refer to a "paternal uncle" due to similar pronunciation rather than meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 我叔爱讲(愛講)笑话(話)。
    - Wǒ shū ài jiǎng xiàohuà.
    - My uncle loves to tell jokes.
  - 我向叔讨(討)教古典文学(學)，他认(認)真地分享经验(經驗)。
    - Wǒ xiàng shū tǎojiào gǔdiǎn wénxué, tā rènzhēn de fēnxiǎng jīngyàn.
    - I sought advice on classical literature from my uncle, and he seriously shared his experience.
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 豆 → 菽 → 叔 → 尗
- **definition:** wooden stake
- **pinyin:** shū
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a wooden stake digging into the dirt
  - **interpretation:** 尗(shū, 'wooden stake') is a pictogram illustrating a simple wooden stake being inserted into the ground, emphasizing its use and design.
### 树(樹) → 尌 → 豆 → 菽 → 叔 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这个字最早来源于手(「又」這個字最早來源於手)。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体现(體現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.

## 死
---
## to die
### sǐ
---
- **definition:** to die
- **pinyin:** sǐ
- **components:**
  - 歹
    - dǎi
    - carcass
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 歹 (dǎi, "carcass") + 人 (rén, "person") =
    - person with remains ->
    - death
  - **interpretation:** The character 死(sǐ, "to die") combines 歹 (dǎi, "carcass") indicating death with 人 (rén, "person") to symbolize a deceased person, highlighting its association with human mortality.
- **examples:**
  - 他的决(決)心大到不怕死。
    - Tā de juéxīn dà dào bù pà sǐ.
    - His determination is so strong that he is not afraid to die.
  - 战场(戰場)上，他见(見)到许(許)多勇士倒下死去。
    - Zhànchǎng shàng, tā jiàndào xǔduō yǒngshì dǎoxià sǐqù.
    - On the battlefield, he saw many brave warriors fall and die.
  - 传说(傳說)中，英雄死后获(後獲)得永生。
    - Chuánshuō zhōng, yīngxióng sǐhòu huòdé yǒngshēng.
    - According to legend, heroes gain eternal life after death.
### 死 → 歹
- **definition:** carcass
- **pinyin:** dǎi
- **components:**
  - 歺
    - è
    - variant form of 歹
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts human remains ->
    - related to 歺 as an intermediate variant
  - **interpretation:** 歹(dǎi, "carcass") is a pictorial representation of human remains. The character preserves an ancient form that visually suggests its meaning, and is related to the intermediate variant 歺.
- **examples:**
  - 他在树(樹)林中发现(發現)一具歹。
    - Tā zài shùlín zhōng fāxiàn yī jù dǎi.
    - He discovered a carcass in the woods.
  - 雨后(後)天晴时(時)，村边(邊)野地露出一具歹。
    - Yǔ hòu tiān qíng shí, cūn biān yě dì lù chū yī jù dǎi.
    - After the rain, when the weather cleared, a carcass appeared on the village outskirts.
### 死 → 歹 → 歺
- **definition:** variant form of 歹
- **pinyin:** è
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts human remains
  - **interpretation:** The character 歺 is a variant form of 歹(dǎi, "bad"), which depicts human remains, conveying an association with death or decay.
### 死 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡献(貢獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵获(靈獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.

## 装(裝)
---
## to pretend; to act as
### zhūang
---
- **traditional:** 裝
- **definition:** to pretend; to act as
- **pinyin:** zhūang
- **components:**
  - 壯
    - zhuàng
    - strong
  - 衣
    - yī
    - clothes
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 壯 (zhuàng, "strong") + 衣 (yī, "clothes") =
    - clothing associated with strength ->
    - to dress or attire
  - **interpretation:** The character 裝 combines 壯, which lends its phonetic value and conveys the notion of strength or robustness, with 衣, indicating clothing. Together, they suggest clothing related to pretending or adopting a role, reflecting how attire can influence perception or facilitate a certain appearance.
  - **simplification:** Clothes radical 衣 was simplified to 衤(衣), preserving key phonetics and semantics while reducing strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他装(裝)作不认识(認識)我，令我感到惊讶(驚訝)。
    - Tā zhuāng zuò bù rènshí wǒ, lìng wǒ gǎndào jīngyà.
    - He pretended not to know me, which surprised me.
  - 她装(裝)出一副高兴(興)的样(樣)子，实则(實則)心中忧虑(憂慮)。
    - Tā zhuāng chū yī fù gāoxìng de yàngzi, shíquè xīnzhōng yōulǜ.
    - She acted as if she were happy, but was actually troubled inside.
  - 他们装(們裝)得很自然。
    - Tāmen zhuāng de hěn zìrán.
    - They acted very naturally.
### 装(裝) → 壯
- **definition:** strong
- **pinyin:** zhuàng
- **components:**
  - 爿
    - pán
    - bedsteads
  - 士
    - shì
    - scholar
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 爿 (pán, "bedsteads") + Semantic: 士 (shì, "scholar") =
    - indicating a scholar's bedding or stature ->
    - strong
  - **interpretation:** In 壯 (zhuàng, "strong"), the component 爿 (pán, "bedsteads") imparts the sound, while 士 (shì, "scholar") suggests the robustness or elevated status of a scholarly person, metaphorically extending to strength.
  - **simplification:** 壮(壯): 士 (shì, "scholar") was simplified to 夂, a less complex shape, while retaining the phonetic and semantic association.
- **examples:**
  - 他很壯。
    - Tā hěn zhuàng.
    - He is very strong.
  - 经过锻炼(經過鍛鍊)，他的肌肉变(變)得更壯。
    - Jīngguò duànliàn, tā de jīròu biàn dé gèng zhuàng.
    - After training, his muscles became even stronger.
  - 古代战(戰)士常被赞颂为(讚頌為)壯志凌云(雲)的英雄。
    - Gǔdài zhànshì cháng bèi zànsòng wéi zhuàngzhì língyún de yīngxióng.
    - Ancient warriors were often praised as heroes with lofty aspirations.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 爿
- **definition:** bedsteads
- **pinyin:** pán
- **components:**
  - 牀
    - chuáng
    - bed
  - 臧
    - zāng
    - favored
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a bed ->
    - Original form of 牀 (chuáng, "bed") ->
    - Contracted form in 臧 (zāng, "favored")
  - **interpretation:** The character 爿(pán, "bed") originally depicted the structure of a bed. It later became the foundational form for the character 牀 (chuáng, "bed") and appears in a contracted form within the character 臧 (zāng, "favored").
- **examples:**
  - 他躺在软软(軟軟)的爿上。
    - Tā tǎng zài ruǎn ruǎn de pán shàng.
    - He lies on the soft bed.
  - 夜深人静时(靜時)，爿边飘(邊飄)散着淡淡的香气(氣)。
    - Yè shēn rén jìng shí, pán biān piāo sàn zhe dàn dàn de xiāng qì.
    - When the night is quiet, a faint fragrance drifts by the bed.
  - 她精心整理过(過)的爿让(讓)人看了舒心。
    - Tā jīngxīn zhěnglǐ guò de pán ràng rén kàn le shūxīn.
    - The bed she meticulously arranged looks very comforting.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 爿 → 牀
- **definition:** bed
- **pinyin:** chuáng
- **components:**
  - 爿(牀)
    - qiáng
    - half of a tree trunk
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 牀 (chuáng, "bed") composed of 爿(牀) (qiáng, "half of a tree trunk") + 木 (mù, "tree") =
    - tree trunk used for support ->
    - bed or wooden bed frame
  - **interpretation:** 牀 (chuáng, "bed") is a phono-semantic compound where 爿(牀) (qiáng, "half of a tree trunk") provides the phonetic element, and 木 (mù, "tree") gives the semantic component, representing its construction from wood.
  - **simplification:** 床 incorporates 广 (guǎng, "house") indicating its placement inside, making 日 (rì, "sun") unnecessary.
- **examples:**
  - 这张牀很舒适(適)。
    - Zhè zhāng chuáng hěn shūshì.
    - This bed is very comfortable.
  - 晚上睡觉时(覺時)，我躺在牀上休息。
    - Wǎnshàng shuìjiào shí, wǒ tǎng zài chuáng shàng xiūxí.
    - When it is time to sleep at night, I lie on the bed to rest.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 爿 → 牀 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 爿 → 臧
- **definition:** favored
- **pinyin:** zāng
- **components:**
  - 臣
    - chén
    - eye
  - 戈
    - gē
    - spear/weapon
  - 爿
    - pán
    - silk panel
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 臣 (chén, "eye") + 戈 (gē, "spear/weapon") =
    - prisoner of war with blinded eyes ->
    - later 爿 (pán) added for phonetic value ->
    - final form 臧
  - **interpretation:** Initially, 臧 depicted a slave or prisoner of war, with the components representing visually inhibited individuals (臣) controlled by force (戈). The character evolved to include a phonetic component 爿, suggesting an additional layer of meaning or a phonetic shift over time.
- **examples:**
  - 他将粮(將糧)食臧在仓库(倉庫)中。
    - Tā jiāng liángshí zāng zài cāngkù zhōng.
    - He stores the grain in the warehouse.
  - 工人先清点(點)物资(資)，后将(將)工具臧于仓(於倉)房。
    - Gōngrén xiān qīngdiǎn wùzī, hòu jiāng gōngjù zāng yú cāngfáng.
    - The workers first count the supplies, then store the tools in the warehouse.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 爿 → 臧 → 臣
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** chén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a vertical eye of a man looking downwards
  - **interpretation:** The character 臣(chén) originally depicted an eye oriented vertically, symbolizing a person looking downwards, conveying subordination or observance. Over time, it evolved to represent roles such as 'slave,' 'servant,' and 'minister,' emphasizing relationships defined by subservience.
- **examples:**
  - 臣愿为国(願為國)家尽(盡)忠。
    - Chén yuàn wèi guójiā jìnzhōng。
    - I, as a loyal subject, am willing to serve the nation faithfully.
  - 陛下召见(見)臣，臣必不辱使命。
    - Bìxià zhàojiàn chén, chén bì bù rǔ shǐmìng。
    - Your Majesty summons me, and I will not fail in my duty.
  - 昔日臣拜见(見)明君，如今仍怀(懷)赤诚(誠)之心。
    - Xīrì chén bàijiàn míngjūn, rújīn réng huái chìchéng zhī xīn。
    - In the past, I paid my respects to a wise ruler, and even now I remain sincerely devoted.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 爿 → 臧 → 戈
- **definition:** spear/weapon
- **pinyin:** gē
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a spear or halberd, a type of weapon
  - **interpretation:** The character 戈(gē, 'spear') visually represents a spear or halberd, highlighting its function and importance as a weapon in ancient Chinese warfare.
- **examples:**
  - 古代战(戰)士持戈，勇闯敌营(闖敵營)。
    - Gǔdài zhànshì chí gē, yǒng chuǎng dí yíng.
    - Ancient warriors wielded the spear, bravely attacking the enemy camp.
  - 博物馆(館)珍藏古兵器，展厅陈(廳陳)列戈。
    - Bówùguǎn zhēncáng gǔ bīngqì, zhǎntīng chénliè gē.
    - The museum preserves ancient weapons, and the exhibition hall displays a spear.
### 装(裝) → 壯 → 士
- **definition:** scholar
- **pinyin:** shì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts an upside-down ritual axe ->
    - later meaning soldier ->
    - eventually officer or intellectual
  - **interpretation:** The character 士 (shì, 'officer') originally depicted a ritual axe, symbolizing authority and power. Over time, it evolved to signify roles associated with leadership and scholarship.
- **examples:**
  - 博物馆今日展出了士，展示古代祭祀器物。
    - Bówùguǎn jīnrì zhǎnchūle shì(士)，zhǎnshì gǔdài jìsì qìwù(展示古代祭祀器物)。
    - The museum exhibited the shì today, showcasing ancient sacrificial vessels.
  - 考古学家在遗址中发现了一把士，被认为(認為)是祭祀用的珍贵(貴)器物。
    - Kǎogǔ xuéjiā zài yízhǐ zhōng fāxiànle yī bǎ shì(士)，bèi rènwéi shì jìsì yòng de zhēnguì qìwù(被認為是祭祀用的珍貴器物)。
    - Archaeologists discovered a shì at the site, which is considered a precious ritual artifact.
  - 工匠精心打造出的士，在阳(陽)光下闪烁(閃爍)着金属(屬)光芒。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn dǎzàochū de shì(士)，zài yángguāng xià shǎnshuò zhe jīnshǔ guāngmáng(在陽光下閃爍着金屬光芒)。
    - The shì, crafted meticulously by artisans, shimmers under the sunlight with a metallic glow.
### 装(裝) → 衣
- **definition:** clothes
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a basic outline of a garment with sleeves hanging down.
  - **interpretation:** The character 衣 (yī, 'clothes') clearly resembles a simple garment, with parts representing sleeves and the body of clothing. This visual representation aligns with its meaning of 'clothes' or 'clothing.'
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)件衣很特别(別)。
    - Zhè jiàn yī hěn tè bié.
    - This piece of clothing is very special.
  - 冬天来(來)了，人们换(們換)上了暖和的衣。
    - Dōngtiān lái le, rénmen huàn shàng le nuǎn huó de yī.
    - Winter has arrived, and people put on warm clothes.

## 装(裝)

## 动(動)
---
## to move
### dòng
---
- **traditional:** 動
- **definition:** to move
- **pinyin:** dòng
- **components:**
  - 力
    - lì
    - strength
  - 重
    - zhòng
    - heavy
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 力 (lì, "strength") + 重 (zhòng, "heavy") =
    - effort applied to shift weight ->
    - move
  - **interpretation:** 力 (lì, "strength") indicates action or exertion of force, while 重 (zhòng, "heavy") serves as a phonetic component capturing the character's pronunciation. Together, they convey the idea of using strength to move or change something.
  - **simplification:** 动(動): Removed 艹 from 重, leaving just another simpler form to represent the sound and meaning.
- **examples:**
  - 他动(動)了动(動)手指，同意了建议(議)。
    - Tā dòngle dòng shǒuzhǐ, tóngyìle jiànyì.
    - He moved his finger and agreed to the suggestion.
  - 心动(動)不已。
    - Xīn dòng bù yǐ.
    - His heart is constantly stirred.
  - 局势频(勢頻)繁动荡(動蕩)，民众(眾)渴望安定。
    - Jú shì pínfán dòng dàng, mínzhòng kěwàng āndìng.
    - The situation is frequently changing, and the people long for stability.
### 动(動) → 力
- **definition:** strength
- **pinyin:** lì
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts either an arm bending out from the side of the body, or a wooden plough
  - **interpretation:** The character 力(lì, 'strength') visually represents physical power through the image of an arm or tool, emphasizing the fundamental concept of muscular force.
- **examples:**
  - 他用尽(盡)全力，赢(贏)得比赛(賽)。
    - Tā yòng jìn quánlì, yíng dé bǐsài.
    - He used all his strength to win the competition.
  - 他把力气(氣)用在学习(學習)上。
    - Tā bǎ lìqì yòng zài xuéxí shàng.
    - He applies his strength to his studies.
  - 面对(對)困难(難)，他毫不退缩(縮)，全力以赴。
    - Miànduì kùnnán, tā háo bù tuìsuō, quánlì yǐ fù.
    - Facing difficulties, he neither retreats nor gives up, but goes all out.
### 动(動) → 重
- **definition:** heavy
- **pinyin:** zhòng
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - man
  - 東
    - dōng
    - bag
  - 土
    - tǔ
    - earth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Phono-semantic compound ( 形聲 / 形声 , OC *doŋ, *doŋʔ, *doŋs ) and ideogrammic compound ( 會意 / 会意 )
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "man") + 東 (dōng, "bag") =
    - a man carrying a bag ->
    - 土 (tǔ, "earth") added to show the bag-carrying man is on the ground ->
    - current form shows heaviness
  - **interpretation:** This character combines the meaning of a person carrying a burden or bag, emphasizing the weight (heavy) of the load, with the semantic reinforcement of standing on the ground. This visually conveys the idea of heaviness.
- **examples:**
  - 这个(這個)箱子很重。
    - Zhège xiāngzi hěn zhòng.
    - This box is very heavy.
  - 我挑水井水时(時)，感觉(覺)瓶子异(異)常重。
    - Wǒ tiāo shuǐjǐng shuǐ shí, gǎnjué píngzi yìcháng zhòng.
    - While I was drawing water from the well, I felt that the bottle was unusually heavy.
### 动(動) → 重 → 人
- **definition:** man
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡献(貢獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵获(靈獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
### 动(動) → 重 → 東
- **definition:** bag
- **pinyin:** dōng
- **components:**
  - 束
    - shù
    - bundle
  - 橐
    - tuó
    - bag
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** Jiajie and ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Originally borrowed from 束 (shù, 'bundle') for sound similarity with 橐 (tuó, 'bag') ->
    - a horizontal stroke added to differentiate 東 (dōng, 'east') ->
    - final form
  - **interpretation:** 東 (dōng) was adapted from existing characters to convey its phonetic sound. It was visually modified to create a unique form, aiding differentiation from related or sound-alike characters.
- **examples:**
  - 我买(買)了个(個)新東。
    - Wǒ mǎi le gè xīn dōng.
    - I bought a new bag.
  - 他把東放在桌上，准备(準備)去旅行。
    - Tā bǎ dōng fàng zài zhuō shàng, zhǔnbèi qù lǚxíng.
    - He put the bag on the table, preparing to travel.
### 动(動) → 重 → 東 → 束
- **definition:** bundle
- **pinyin:** shù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bundle of sticks tied together
  - **interpretation:** The character 束 (shù, 'bundle') visually represents a group of items, such as sticks or reeds, that have been gathered and tied tightly together. This depiction is direct and intuitive for conveying the idea of a bundle.
- **examples:**
  - 他拎着(著)一束鲜(鮮)花。
    - Tā līn zhe yī shù xiānhuā.
    - He is carrying a bundle of fresh flowers.
  - 园(園)丁修剪完花朵后(後)，将(將)它们(們)整理成一束。
    - Yuándīng xiūjiǎn wán huāduǒ hòu, jiāng tāmen zhěnglǐ chéng yī shù.
    - After trimming the flowers, the gardener arranged them into a bundle.
  - 小贩(販)把蔬菜捆成一束，然后(後)去市场(場)出售。
    - Xiǎofàn bǎ shūcài kǔn chéng yī shù, ránhòu qù shìchǎng chūshòu.
    - The vendor bundled the vegetables and then went to the market to sell them.
### 动(動) → 重 → 東 → 橐
- **definition:** bag
- **pinyin:** tuó
- **components:**
  - 𣒚
    - n/a
    - bag with a bottom
  - 石
    - shí
    - stone
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 𣒚 (depicts a bag with a bottom) + 石 (shí, 'stone') as phonetic =
    - bag-like object ->
    - concept of 'bag'
  - **interpretation:** The character 橐 combines the semantic element 𣒚, which originally depicted a bag with a distinct bottom, with 石 (shí, 'stone') to convey the sound. The character represents the concept of a 'bag' by visually incorporating the shape of a bag and using 石 to aid pronunciation.
- **examples:**
  - 他把珍贵(貴)的卷轴(軸)放进(進)橐里(裡)。
    - tā bǎ zhēnguì de juǎnzhóu fàng jìn tuó lǐ.
    - He put the precious scroll into the bag.
  - 晋(晉)朝文人描绘(繪)官员携(員攜)橐归来(歸來)。
    - jìn cháo wénrén miáohuì guānyuán xié tuó guī lái.
    - Literati from the Jin Dynasty depicted officials returning with the bag.
  - 他的小橐装满(裝滿)了长(長)江水，激起了浪花。
    - tā de xiǎo tuó zhuāng mǎn le chángjiāng shuǐ, jī qǐ le lànghuā.
    - His small bag was filled with water from the Yangtze, splashing into waves.
### 动(動) → 重 → 東 → 橐 → 𣒚
- **definition:** bag with a bottom
- **pinyin:** n/a
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a bag with a distinctive bottom
  - **interpretation:** The character 𣒚 visually represents a bag or sack with a defined bottom section, indicating its functional use as a container.
### 动(動) → 重 → 東 → 橐 → 石
- **definition:** stone
- **pinyin:** shí
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stone beneath a cliff, where the upper part originally looked like a cliff (厂) but was distorted into 丆 over time.
  - **interpretation:** The character 石(shí, 'stone') visually represents a stone in a natural setting, highlighting the element of a cliff or mountain. Its visual design aims to reflect the appearance of rocks lodged or embedded in a mountainous or cliff-like setting.
- **examples:**
  - 他在河边发现(邊發現)一块(塊)石。
    - Tā zài hé biān fāxiàn yī kuài shí.
    - He discovered a piece of stone by the riverside.
  - 孩子们(們)喜欢(歡)堆石，玩得开(開)心。
    - Háizimen xǐhuān duī shí, wán de kāixīn.
    - Children like to stack stones, playing happily.
### 动(動) → 重 → 土
- **definition:** earth
- **pinyin:** tǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound of earth
  - **interpretation:** The character 土(tǔ, "earth") visually represents a mound or piece of land, with a horizontal line indicating the surface and a vertical line the height of the mound. It's a straightforward depiction of earth or soil.
- **examples:**
  - 农(農)民耕土，种(種)出丰(豐)收。
    - Nóngmín gēng tǔ, zhòng chū fēngshōu.
    - Farmers cultivate the earth and harvest abundantly.
  - 院子里(裡)的土，适(適)合种(種)花。
    - Yuànzi lǐ de tǔ, shìhé zhòng huā.
    - The soil in the yard is suitable for planting flowers.
