## 危( )险(險)
---
## dangerous
### wēixiǎn
---
- **traditional:** 危險
- **definition:** dangerous
- **pinyin:** wēixiǎn
- **components:**
  - 危
    - wēi
    - dangerous; high; steep; critical
  - 险(險)
    - xiǎn
    - danger; risk; hazard; peril
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 危 (wēi, "dangerous") + 險 (xiǎn, "danger") =
    - a state of danger or risk
  - **interpretation:** 危險 (wēixiǎn, "dangerous") describes a situation that involves a high degree of risk or the potential for harm. The combination of 危 (wēi, "dangerous") and 險 (xiǎn, "danger") emphasizes the seriousness and potential threat inherent in such circumstances.
- **examples:**
  - 这里(這裡)很危险(險)。
    - Zhèlǐ hěn wēixiǎn.
    - It is dangerous here.
  - 那条(條)路很危险(險)，许(許)多人避而远(遠)之。
    - Nà tiáo lù hěn wēixiǎn, xǔduō rén bì ér yuǎn zhī.
    - That road is very dangerous, so many people avoid it.
### 危( )险(險) → 危
- **definition:** dangerous; high; steep; critical
- **pinyin:** wēi
- **components:**
  - 懸
    - xuán
    - hang
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** variant form
  - **description:** 危 (wēi, "dangerous") is a variant form of 懸 (xuán, "hang")
  - **interpretation:** The character 危 (wēi, "dangerous") is understood as a variant form of 懸 (xuán, "hang"), emphasizing the meanings of danger and critical situations, derived from the notion of things hanging or suspended, which inherently carry risk.
- **examples:**
  - 山势险(勢險)峻，情况(況)危急。
    - Shān shì xiǎnjùn(Shān shì xiǎnjùn)，qíngkuàng wēijí(qíngkuàng wēijí)。
    - The mountain terrain is steep, and the situation is critical.
  - 那条(條)山路又危又陡。
    - Nà tiáo shānlù yòu wēi yòu dǒu(Nà tiáo shānlù yòu wēi yòu dǒu)。
    - That mountain road is both dangerous and steep.
  - 船行急流时(時)，处(處)境非常危。
    - Chuán xíng jíliú shí(Chuán xíng jíliú shí)，chǔjìng fēicháng wēi(Chǔjìng fēicháng wēi)。
    - When the boat sails in rapid currents, its situation is extremely dangerous.
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸
- **definition:** hang
- **pinyin:** xuán
- **components:**
  - 縣
    - xuán
    - county
  - 心
    - xīn
    - heart
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 縣 (xuán) (phonetic, 'county') + 心 (xīn, 'heart') =
    - originally 縣 also meant 'to hang'; 心 added for distinction ->
    - 懸('hang')
  - **interpretation:** The character 懸(xuán) combines the phonetic element 縣 (xuán, 'county') with the semantic element 心 (xīn, 'heart'). The original character 縣 encompassed the meaning 'to hang,' and 心 was added to distinguish this meaning from 'county', resulting in 懸 for 'hang'.
  - **simplification:** 悬(懸): The simplified form removes the 心 (xīn, 'heart') component, streamlining the complex phono-semantic compound.
- **examples:**
  - 他把画悬(畫懸)在墙(牆)上。
    - Tā bǎ huà xuán zài qiáng shàng.
    - He hangs the painting on the wall.
  - 树(樹)枝上悬着风铃(懸著風鈴)，微风(風)拂过(過)枝头(頭)。
    - Shù zhī shàng xuán zhe fēng líng, wēi fēng fú guò zhī tóu.
    - Wind chimes hang on the branches, and a gentle breeze brushes through the boughs.
  - 古城桥(橋)上悬挂着(懸掛著)彩灯(燈)。
    - Gǔ chéng qiáo shàng xuán guà zhe cǎi dēng.
    - Colorful lanterns hang on the ancient city bridge.
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 縣
- **definition:** county
- **pinyin:** xuán
- **components:**
  - 目
    - mù
    - eye
  - 木
    - mù
    - tree
  - 糸
    - sī
    - string
  - 懸
    - xuán
    - to hang
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 目 (mù, "eye/head") + 木 (mù, "tree") + 糸 (sī, "string") =
    - hanging a head by string on a tree ->
    - referred to 懸(xuán, "to hang") ->
    - later borrowed for 縣 (xuán, "county")
  - **interpretation:** The character 縣 originally depicted the head (eye) being hung by a string on a tree, symbolizing the action of hanging. This character was later borrowed for administrative divisions, likely due to the phonetic similarity to 懸(xuán, "to hang"). Over time, the original representation was adapted and corrupted, but the connotations of oversight and governance (like an overseer hanging over an area) may have influenced its adoption for 'county.'
  - **simplification:** The traditional character 縣 was simplified to 县 by removing 糸 (sī, "string") and simplifying the components for ease of writing, while retaining phonetic aspects.
- **examples:**
  - 我住在一个(個)小县(縣)。
    - Wǒ zhù zài yīgè xiǎo xuán.
    - I live in a small county.
  - 他访问(訪問)了古老的县(縣)，体验(體驗)了乡(鄉)村风(風)情。
    - Tā fǎngwèn le gǔlǎo de xuán, tǐyàn le xiāngcūn fēngqíng.
    - He visited an ancient county and experienced the rural customs.
  - 他们骑车(們騎車)穿过县(過縣)城，感受了悠久的文化。
    - Tāmen qí chē chuānguò xuánchéng, gǎnshòu le yōujiǔ de wénhuà.
    - They rode bicycles through the county town and experienced its long-standing culture.
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 縣 → 目
- **definition:** eye
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a human eye, now represented and rotated 90 degrees ->
    - eye
  - **interpretation:** The character 目(mù, 'eye') is a pictogram representing a human eye. Its original orientation has changed over time, resembling an eye seen from a sideways view.
- **examples:**
  - 他的目光炯炯有神。
    - Tā de mùguāng jiǒngjiǒng yǒu shén.
    - His gaze is bright and full of spirit.
  - 她目不转(轉)睛，注视(視)前方。
    - Tā mù bù zhuǎn jīng, zhùshì qiánfāng.
    - She stared intently, gazing ahead.
  - 雄鹰(鷹)展翅，双(雙)目炯炯看天际(際)。
    - Xióng yīng zhǎn chì, shuāng mù jiǒngjiǒng kàn tiānjì.
    - The eagle spreads its wings, its eyes piercingly gaze at the horizon.
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 縣 → 木
- **definition:** tree
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 縣 → 糸
- **definition:** string
- **pinyin:** sī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a skein of silk
  - **interpretation:** The character 糸(mì, "silk; thread") represents a pictorial representation of a skein of silk, visually capturing the concept of thread or fiber.
- **examples:**
  - 她手工制(製)作了一条(條)漂亮的丝(絲)巾。
    - Tā shǒugōng zhìzuòle yī tiáo piàoliang de sī jīn.
    - She handcrafted a beautiful silk scarf.
  - 这个设计图(這個設計圖)必须(須)用细(細)糸画(畫)出来(來)。
    - Zhège shèjìtú bìxū yòng xì mì huà chūlái.
    - This design drawing must be sketched with fine thread.
  - 我们参观(們參觀)了古代的织(織)布技术(術)，对丝绸制(對絲綢製)作产(產)生了兴(興)趣。
    - Wǒmen cānguānle gǔdài de zhībù jìshù, duì sīchóu zhìzuò chǎnshēngle xìngqù.
    - We visited ancient weaving techniques and developed an interest in silk production.
### 危( )险(險) → 危 → 懸 → 心
- **definition:** heart
- **pinyin:** xīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stylized representation of a heart
  - **interpretation:** The character 心(xīn, 'heart') visually represents the shape of a heart, emphasizing its central and essential role in both a physical and metaphorical sense.
- **examples:**
  - 他的心温(溫)暖无(無)比。
    - Tā de xīn wēnnuǎn wúbǐ.
    - His heart is incredibly warm.
  - 她把心放在艺术(藝術)上，追求完美。
    - Tā bǎ xīn fàng zài yìshù shàng, zhuīqiú wánměi.
    - She dedicates her heart to art, pursuing perfection.
  - 音乐(樂)直击(擊)心灵(靈)。
    - Yīnyuè zhí jī xīnlíng.
    - Music strikes straight at the heart (soul).
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險)
- **traditional:** 險
- **definition:** danger; risk; hazard; peril
- **pinyin:** xiǎn
- **components:**
  - 阝(阜)
    - fù
    - mound
  - 僉
    - qiān
    - gather
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 阝(阜) (fù, "mound") + phonetic: 僉 (qiān) =
    - resembling a mound or high ground + phonetic value ->
    - danger or risk
  - **interpretation:** The character 險 (xiǎn, "danger") combines the element 阝(阜) (fù, "mound"), suggesting something elevated or protruding like a hill, and the phonetic 僉 (qiān), which provides the pronunciation and implies a sense of accumulation or incorporation, thus together indicating a place or situation that poses potential threat or difficulty due to its terrain or circumstances.
  - **simplification:** 險 was simplified to 险(險) by changing the left-side 阝(阜) to its common simplified form 阝(阜), while retaining the phonetic component 僉; however, 阝 represents a simplified version of the original with fewer strokes.
- **examples:**
  - 他决(決)定冒险(險)一试(試)。
    - Tā juédìng màoxiǎn yī shì.
    - He decided to take the risk and give it a try.
  - 驾驶时(駕駛時)要小心，避免不必要的险(險)情。
    - Jiàshǐ shí yào xiǎoxīn, bìmiǎn bù bìyào de xiǎnqíng.
    - Drive carefully to avoid unnecessary dangers.
  - 探险(險)家穿越原始森林时(時)，面临着(臨著)未知的险(險)境。
    - Tànxiǎnjiā chuānyuè yuánshǐ sēnlín shí, miànlínzhe wéizhī de xiǎnjìng.
    - The explorer, while traversing the primeval forest, faced unknown hazards.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 阝
- **definition:** mound
- **pinyin:** fù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a small mound or hillock.
  - **interpretation:** The character 阝 (fù, 'mound') visually represents a small elevation of land, resembling a hillside or embankment.
- **examples:**
  - 小山顶(頂)上耸(聳)立着阝(著阜)。
    - Xiǎo shāndǐng shàng sǒnglì zhe fù.
    - A small mound stands atop the hill.
  - 山坡上长满(長滿)了绿(綠)色的草丛(叢)，山丘边(邊)坐落着(著)一座古老的阝(阜)。
    - Shānpō shàng cháng mǎn le lǜsè de cǎocóng, shānqiū biān zuòluò zhe yī zuò gǔlǎo de fù.
    - The hillside is covered with green grass, and an ancient mound sits by the hill.
  - 远处(遠處)沙丘边隐约(邊隱約)可见(見)一堆阝(阜)，仿佛历(彷彿歷)史的见证(見證)。
    - Yuǎnchù shāqiū biān yǐnyuē kějiàn yī duī fù, fǎngfú lìshǐ de jiànzhèng.
    - In the distance, a pile of mounds is barely visible by the sand dunes, as if witnessing history.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉
- **definition:** gather
- **pinyin:** qiān
- **components:**
  - 亼
    - jié
    - to gather
  - 兄
    - xiōng
    - elder brother
  - 吅
    - xuān
    - multiple mouths
  - 从(從)
    - cóng
    - to follow
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 亼 (jié, "to gather") + 兄 (xiōng, "elder brother") repeated ->
    - people answering to a call together ->
    - stylized as 亼 + 吅 (multiple mouths) + 从 (cóng, "to follow")
  - **interpretation:** The character 僉 originally depicted two elder brothers gathered under one roof, symbolizing a group consensus or collective agreement. Over time, it evolved to use figurative components for collective actions and agreements, represented by voices and followers.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 亼
- **definition:** to gather
- **pinyin:** jié
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 入 (rù, "enter") + 一 (yī, "one") =
    - gather from three sides
  - **interpretation:** 9.61
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)幅画(畫)描绘(繪)了亼的独(獨)特形状(狀)。
    - Zhè fú huà miáohuì le jī de dú tè xíngzhuàng.
    - This painting depicts the unique shape of 亼, resembling an open mouth flipped upside down.
  - 古籍记载(記載)亼符号(號)的古怪寓意，令后(後)人赞叹(讚嘆)不已。
    - Gǔ jí jì zǎi jī fú hào de gǔ guài yù yì, lìng hòu rén zàn tàn bù yǐ.
    - Ancient texts record the bizarre symbolism of 亼, which inspires endless admiration from later generations.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 兄
- **definition:** elder brother
- **pinyin:** xiōng
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
  - 儿
    - ér
    - child
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + 儿 (ér, "child") =
    - giving orders ->
    - elder brother
  - **interpretation:** The character 兄 (xiōng, "brother") combines 口 (kǒu, "mouth") with 儿 (ér, "child") to depict an elder brother who gives orders. This conveys the traditional family role of the elder brother as a figure of authority, similar to other characters like 令 (lìng, "order") that emphasize the act of speaking or commanding.
- **examples:**
  - 我兄从(從)小向我传(傳)授智慧，使我终(終)生受益。
    - wǒ xiōng cóng xiǎo xiàng wǒ chuánshòu zhìhuì, shǐ wǒ zhōngshēng shòuyì.
    - My brother taught me wisdom from childhood, which has benefited me all my life.
  - 贤(賢)兄常助我困境。
    - xián xiōng cháng zhù wǒ kùn jìng.
    - My worthy brother often helps me overcome difficulties.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 兄 → 口
- **definition:** mouth
- **pinyin:** kǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts an open mouth.
  - **interpretation:** The character 口(kǒu, 'mouth') is a straightforward pictogram that visually represents an open mouth. It is a fundamental character in the Chinese language, often used both as an independent word and as a component in more complex characters, lending a semantic association to ideas relating to speech, openings, or enclosures.
- **examples:**
  - 他张开(張開)口，大声(聲)喊叫。
    - Tā zhāngkāi kǒu, dàshēng hǎnjiào.
    - He opened his mouth and shouted loudly.
  - 这(這)口饭(飯)入口即化。
    - Zhè kǒu fàn rùkǒu jíhuà.
    - This mouthful of food melts in your mouth.
  - 小女孩咬了一口苹(蘋)果，露出甜美的笑容。
    - Xiǎo nǚhái yǎole yī kǒu píngguǒ, lùchū tiánměi de xiàoróng.
    - The little girl took a bite of the apple and smiled sweetly.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 兄 → 儿(兒)
- **traditional:** 兒
- **definition:** child
- **pinyin:** ér
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a person standing upright, showing legs
  - **interpretation:** The character 儿(兒) (ér) originally represents a stylized depiction of a person, particularly emphasizing the legs as if they are walking or standing. This provides a visual representation of the concept 'person'.
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)勇敢的儿(兒)。
    - Tā shì gè yǒnggǎn de ér.
    - He is a brave person.
  - 村里有一个(個)勤劳(勞)的儿(兒)，总帮(總幫)助邻(鄰)居解决问题(決問題)。
    - Cūn lǐ yǒu yī gè qínláo de ér, zǒng bāngzhù línjū jiějué wèntí.
    - There is a hardworking person in the village, who always helps neighbors solve problems.
  - 古城中流传着(傳著)一位智者儿(兒)，他的故事激励后(勵後)人。
    - Gǔ chéng zhōng liúchuán zhe yī wèi zhìzhě de ér, tā de gùshì jīlì hòurén.
    - In the ancient city, the story of a wise person is passed down, and his tale inspires future generations.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 吅
- **definition:** multiple mouths
- **pinyin:** xuān
- **components:**
  - 口
    - kǒu
    - mouth
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 口 (kǒu, "mouth") + 口 (kǒu, "mouth") =
    - multiple mouths ->
    - 吅
  - **interpretation:** The character 吅(xuān) is an ideogrammic compound that visually represents the concept of 'multiple mouths,' using two instances of 口 (kǒu, "mouth") stacked together to convey multiplicity or a loud expression. This composition makes intuitive sense as it uses repetition to signify 'many mouths,' implying the idea of numerous people speaking or shouting together.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從)
- **traditional:** 從
- **definition:** to follow
- **pinyin:** cóng
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 辵
    - chuò
    - walk
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") duplicated + 辵 (chuò, "walk") as semantic =
    - following people walking together ->
    - "follow"; phonetic: 从(cong, "follow")
  - **interpretation:** The character 从(cóng, "from") visually depicts two people walking in the same direction, symbolizing following someone. In its traditional form, 從(cong, "follow") added the "walk" radical to reinforce the idea of movement and accompaniment.
  - **simplification:** 从 was retained as a shorthand for 從 by omitting the 辵 (chuò, "walk") radical, preserving its original depiction of two people walking.
- **examples:**
  - 我从学(從學)校回来(來)。
    - Wǒ cóng xuéxiào huílái.
    - I returned from school.
  - 他从乡(從鄉)村出发(發)，前往都市。
    - Tā cóng xiāngcūn chūfā, qiánwǎng dūshì.
    - He set off from the countryside, heading to the city.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從) → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡献(貢獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵获(靈獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從) → 辵
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** chuò
- **components:**
  - 彳
    - chì
    - walk
  - 止
    - zhǐ
    - foot
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 彳 (chì, "walk") + 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop") ->
    - 𣥆 ->
    - stylized as 龰 ->
    - 辵
  - **interpretation:** The character 辵 combines 彳 (chì, "walk"), which represents movement, with 止 (zhǐ, "foot" or "to stop"), suggesting the concept of stepping or traveling forward. This character represents the idea of movement, particularly the action of walking or traveling, as originally depicted by the more conservative form 𣥆. Over time, the bottom component has been stylized as 龰, forming the current representation.
- **examples:**
  - 他辵在乡间(鄉間)的小路上。
    - Tā chuò zài xiāngjiān de xiǎolù shàng.
    - He walks on the rural path.
  - 晨光洒满(灑滿)大地，他辵出门开(門開)始旅程。
    - Chén guāng sǎ mǎn dàdì, tā chuò chūmén kāishǐ lǚchéng.
    - As the morning light fills the earth, he sets out to begin his journey.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從) → 辵 → 彳
- **definition:** walk
- **pinyin:** chì
- **components:**
  - 行
    - xíng
    - go
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts 街 intersection viewed from above, simplified from 行 (xíng, "go")
  - **interpretation:** The character 彳(chì, "walking") represents the image of a street intersection, which symbolically indicates movement or walking. It is used to denote the concept of going or moving along a path.
- **examples:**
  - 他彳亍而行。
    - Tā chìchù ér xíng.
    - He ambled along slowly.
  - 老人彳步，穿过(過)小巷。
    - Lǎorén chì bù, chuānguò xiǎoxiàng.
    - The old man walked along, crossing the narrow alley.
  - 孩子们(們)看到蝴蝶，便兴奋(興奮)地彳走前去。
    - Háizimen kàn dào húdié, biàn xīngfèn de chì zǒu qiánqù.
    - Upon seeing the butterflies, the children excitedly walked forward.
### 危( )险(險) → 险(險) → 僉 → 从(從) → 辵 → 止
- **definition:** foot
- **pinyin:** zhǐ
- **components:**
  - 趾
    - zhǐ
    - foot
  - 龰
    - yù
    - stylized feet
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Original: Foot pointing up with 3 toes and a sole ->
    - Stylized as 龰 ->
    - Derivative 趾 refers to original 'foot' meaning
  - **interpretation:** Originally depicting a footprint with toes and a sole, 止 (zhǐ, "foot") represents the foot. The character's form resembles a foot with three toes, analogous to how the hand is represented with fingers in other characters.
- **examples:**
  - 他受伤(傷)的止需要静养(靜養)。
    - Tā shòu shāng de zhǐ xū yào jìng yǎng.
    - His injured foot needs adequate rest.
  - 他走路时(時)小心谨(謹)慎，因为(爲)止若受伤(傷)便难(難)前行。
    - Tā zǒu lù shí xiǎo xīn jǐn shèn, yīn wèi zhǐ ruò shòu shāng biàn nán qián xíng.
    - He walks carefully because if his foot gets injured, it becomes difficult to move forward.
---
## 危( )险(險)
### wēixiǎn

## 条(條)
---
## strip; long narrow piece; measure word for long objects
### tiáo
---
- **traditional:** 條
- **definition:** strip; long narrow piece; measure word for long objects
- **pinyin:** tiáo
- **components:**
  - 攸
    - yōu
    - distant
  - 木
    - mù
    - wood
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 攸 (yōu, "distant") + Semantic: 木 (mù, "wood") =
    - small branch reference ->
    - strip or item
  - **interpretation:** The character 條 (tiáo, "strip; item") combines the phonetic element 攸 (yōu, "distant") with the semantic 木 (mù, "wood") to convey the idea of a wooden strip or item. This aligns with its meaning related to strips or items made of wood.
  - **simplification:** 条(條) uses a similar top component 攸 from 條, with a simplified overall structure but retains phonetic and semantic references.
- **examples:**
  - 我买(買)了一条(條)裙子。
    - Wǒ mǎi le yī tiáo qúnzi.
    - I bought a skirt.
  - 他在公园(園)看到一条(條)蜥蜴，迅速跑开(開)。
    - Tā zài gōngyuán kàn dào yī tiáo xīyì, xùnsù pǎokāi.
    - He saw a lizard in the park and ran away quickly.
  - 这(這)本小说(說)分为(為)五条(條)故事线(線)，各自精彩纷(紛)呈。
    - Zhè běn xiǎoshuō fēnwéi wǔ tiáo gùshì xiàn, gèzì jīngcǎi fēnchéng.
    - This novel is divided into five storylines, each wonderfully exciting.
### 条(條) → 攸
- **definition:** distant
- **pinyin:** yōu
- **components:**
  - 人
    - rén
    - person
  - 攴
    - pū
    - to tap; to strike
  - 水
    - shuǐ
    - water
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 人 (rén, "person") + 攴 (pū, "to tap; to strike") + suggested 水 (shuǐ, "water") dots ->
    - act of pouring water on a person as purification or warning
  - **interpretation:** The character 攸(yōu, "distant") combines 人 (rén, "person") indicating a person, with 攴 (pū, "to tap; to strike") suggesting authority or purification through symbolic action. The added component of 水 (shuǐ, "water") emphasizes a ceremonial context, hinting at purification or ritual warning.
### 条(條) → 攸 → 人
- **definition:** person
- **pinyin:** rén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts side view of a standing man, highlighting an arm and a leg ->
    - visual representation of a person
  - **interpretation:** The character 人 (rén, 'person') effectively uses simple lines to depict the essential form of a human, making it immediately recognizable and intuitive as meaning 'person.'
- **examples:**
  - 他是个(個)好人。
    - Tā shì gè hǎo rén.
    - He is a good person.
  - 每个(個)人都有责(責)任，为(為)社会(會)作出贡献(貢獻)。
    - Měi gè rén dōu yǒu zérèn, wèi shèhuì zuòchū gòngxiàn.
    - Every person has a responsibility to contribute to society.
  - 人在旅途中，心灵获(靈獲)得了成长(長)。
    - Rén zài lǚtú zhōng, xīnlíng huòdé le chéngzhǎng.
    - People gain growth along their journey.
### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴
- **definition:** to tap; to strike
- **pinyin:** pū
- **components:**
  - 手
    - shǒu
    - hand
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
  - 卜
    - bǔ
    - divine
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - 手 (shǒu, 'hand') depicted as 又 (yòu, 'hand') holding a tool ->
    - later stylized to look like 卜 (bǔ, 'divine') ->
    - simplified further
  - **interpretation:** The character 攴 originally depicted a hand holding a tool, possibly implying action such as hitting. Over time, for stylistic reasons, it was modified to resemble the component 卜, even though the phonetic aspect was retained.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手指攴轻(輕)叩鼓面，传递(傳遞)出节(節)奏的信号(號)。
    - Tā yòng shǒuzhǐ pū le qīng kòu gǔmiàn, chuándì chū jiézòu de xìnhào.
    - He tapped the drum surface lightly with his finger, conveying the rhythm's signal.
  - 她突然攴了一下门(門)，唤(喚)起了室内(內)的安静(靜)。
    - Tā túrán pū le yīxià mén, huànqǐ le shìnèi de ānjìng.
    - She suddenly tapped the door, awakening the quiet inside.
### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 手
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** shǒu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a hand with fingers; top stroke is a bent over middle finger, horizontal strokes represent fingers
  - **interpretation:** The character 手 (shǒu, "hand") is a direct pictorial representation of a human hand with all five fingers, which distinguishes it from similar characters representing claws or simplified fingers. This visually conveys its meaning as a hand clearly.
- **examples:**
  - 他用手写(寫)字。
    - Tā yòng shǒu xiě zì.
    - He writes with his hand.
  - 妈妈牵着(媽媽牽著)我的手走路。
    - Māmā qiān zhe wǒ de shǒu zǒu lù.
    - Mom holds my hand while walking.
  - 他的手很温(溫)暖，带给(帶給)我力量。
    - Tā de shǒu hěn wēn nuǎn, dài gěi wǒ lìliàng.
    - His hand is very warm, giving me strength.
### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这个字最早来源于手(「又」這個字最早來源於手)。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体现(體現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
### 条(條) → 攸 → 攴 → 卜
- **definition:** divine
- **pinyin:** bǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a divination crack in a tortoise shell or bone
  - **interpretation:** The character 卜(bǔ, "divination") represents the practice of divination used in ancient China, often involving the interpretation of cracks in tortoise shells or bones.
- **examples:**
  - 占卜是一种(種)神秘的艺术(藝術)。
    - Zhānbǔ shì yī zhǒng shénmì de yìshù.
    - Divination is a mysterious art.
  - 他通过(過)卜算未来(來)，探寻隐(尋隱)秘的命运(運)。
    - Tā tōngguò bǔsuàn wèilái, tànxún yǐnmì de mìngyùn.
    - He uses divination to predict the future, seeking out his hidden destiny.
  - 古代人常以卜问(問)吉凶，以求平安和顺(順)。
    - Gǔdài rén cháng yǐ bǔ wèn jíxiōng, yǐ qiú píng'ān hé shùn.
    - Ancient people often practiced divination to determine fortune, in order to pursue peace and order.
### 条(條) → 攸 → 水
- **definition:** water
- **pinyin:** shuǐ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flowing water
  - **interpretation:** 水 (shuǐ, 'water') is a pictogram that directly represents the appearance of flowing water, making it intuitive and easy to recognize. Its simplicity and direct visual reference to its meaning have allowed it to remain unchanged over millennia.
- **examples:**
  - 水是一种(種)生命之源。
    - Shuǐ shì yī zhǒng shēngmìng zhī yuán.
    - Water is the source of life.
  - 夏天很热(熱)，喝水能解暑。
    - Xiàtiān hěn rè, hē shuǐ néng jiě shǔ.
    - It is very hot in summer, drinking water can relieve the heat.
  - 河水潺潺，沿岸绿树(綠樹)成荫(蔭)。
    - Hé shuǐ chánchán, yán'àn lǜshù chéng yīn.
    - The river flows babbling, and green trees along the bank provide shade.
### 条(條) → 木
- **definition:** wood
- **pinyin:** mù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a tree with branches and roots
  - **interpretation:** The character 木(mù) depicts a tree, showing the trunk in the center and two slanting lines representing branches or roots. It directly signifies the concept of wood or a tree.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)把椅子的主要材料是木。
    - Zhè bǎ yǐzi de zhǔyào cáiliào shì mù.
    - The main material of this chair is wood.
  - 工匠精心雕刻木，制成精美家具。
    - Gōngjiàng jīngxīn diāo kè mù, zhìchéng jīngměi jiājù.
    - The craftsman carefully carved the wood, crafting exquisite furniture.
---
## 条(條)
### tiáo

## 龙(龍)
---
## dragon
### lóng
---
- **traditional:** 龍
- **definition:** dragon
- **pinyin:** lóng
- **components:**
  - 辰
    - chén
    - early form of dragon
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 辰 (chén, "early form of dragon") as phonetic + stylized depiction of a dragon body =
    - 龙 ->
    - dragon
  - **interpretation:** 龙(龍) (lóng, "dragon") combines a phonetic element from 辰 (chén, "early form of dragon") with a stylized representation of a dragon's body, capturing both sound and essence to represent the mythical creature.
  - **simplification:** 龙(龍) simplified by combining phonetic 辰 with a less detailed body form to represent the dragon.
- **examples:**
  - 传说(傳說)中的龙(龍)能呼风唤(風喚)雨。
    - Chuánshuō zhōng de lóng néng hū fēng huàn yǔ.
    - The legendary dragon can summon wind and rain.
  - 皇宫(宮)中悬挂着龙(懸掛著龍)袍，象征着(徵著)至高无(無)上的权(權)力。
    - Huánggōng zhōng xuánguà zhe lóng páo, xiàngzhēng zhe zhìgāo wúshàng de quánlì.
    - In the imperial palace, the dragon robe hangs, symbolizing supreme power.
### 龙(龍) → 辰
- **definition:** early form of dragon
- **pinyin:** chén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heavenly body or a celestial presence, often associated with dragons in ancient mythology.
  - **interpretation:** 辰 (chén, "early form of dragon") originally depicted a celestial body that was believed to influence time and was associated with dragons due to mythological links between dragons and celestial phenomena.
- **examples:**
  - 古代传说(傳說)中的辰是神秘而强(強)大的生物。
    - Gǔdài chuánshuō zhōng de chén shì shénmì ér qiángdà de shēngwù.
    - In ancient legends, the chén is a mysterious and powerful creature.
  - 东(東)方初升的朝阳(陽)映照着(著)辰的鳞(鱗)光，唤(喚)起了古老的神话(話)。
    - Dōngfāng chūshēng de cháoyáng yìngzhào zhe chén de línguāng, huànqǐ le gǔlǎo de shénhuà.
    - The rising morning sun in the east illuminates the scales of the chén, evoking ancient myths.
  - 传(傳)承了古老智慧的文献记载(獻記載)了辰的奇迹(蹟)，使后(後)人对(對)它充满(滿)敬畏。
    - Chuánchéng le gǔlǎo zhìhuì de wénxiàn jìzǎi le chén de qíjī, shǐ hòurén duì tā chōngmǎn jìngwèi.
    - Ancient texts carrying old wisdom recorded the miracles of the chén, filling later generations with awe.
---
## 龙(龍)
### lóng
---
## dragon

## 拍
---
## to pat; to beat; to take (a picture)
### pāi
---
- **definition:** to pat; to beat; to take (a picture)
- **pinyin:** pāi
- **components:**
  - 骨
    - gǔ
    - bone
  - 尃
    - fū
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 骨 (gǔ, "bone") + 尃 (fū) =
    - semantic + phonetic elements
  - **interpretation:** Originally, 拍 was an obsolete form of 髆, where it combined the semantic element 骨 (gǔ, "bone") with the phonetic element 尃 (fū). The character has evolved to mean 'to pat' or 'to take a picture,' likely due to the action of tapping or hitting lightly, similar to the precision and care in focusing a camera.
- **examples:**
  - 妈妈轻轻(媽媽輕輕)拍我的肩膀。
    - Māmā qīngqīng pāi wǒ de jiānbǎng.
    - Mom gently patted my shoulder.
  - 我们(們)去公园(園)，拍美丽(麗)的风(風)景。
    - Wǒmen qù gōngyuán, pāi měilì de fēngjǐng.
    - We go to the park to take pictures of the beautiful scenery.
  - 他生气(氣)地拍桌子。
    - Tā shēngqì de pāi zhuōzi.
    - He angrily banged on the table.
### 拍 → 骨
- **definition:** bone
- **pinyin:** gǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts the human spine and ribs, resembling a skeletal structure.
  - **interpretation:** The character 骨 (gǔ, "bone") visually represents the shape and layout of a human spine and ribs.
- **examples:**
  - 这(這)根骨很坚(堅)硬。
    - Zhè gēn gǔ hěn jiānyìng.
    - This bone is very hard.
  - 老中医观(醫觀)察骨的脉络(脈絡)，寻(尋)找健康之秘。
    - Lǎo zhōngyī guānchá gǔ de màiluò, xúnzhǎo jiànkāng zhī mì.
    - The experienced Chinese doctor examines the bone structure to seek the secret of health.
### 拍 → 尃
- **pinyin:** fū
- **components:**
  - 甫
    - fǔ
    - garden
  - 寸
    - cùn
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Phonetic: 甫 (fǔ, 'garden') + Semantic: 寸 (cùn, 'hand') ->
    - to distribute crops
  - **interpretation:** The character 尃 combines the phonetic element 甫 (fǔ, 'garden') with the semantic element 寸 (cùn, 'hand') to depict the action of distributing or spreading crops with the hand. This illustrates an agricultural context, reflecting how crops need to be evenly distributed across a field.
### 拍 → 尃 → 甫
- **definition:** garden
- **pinyin:** fǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a broad field, originally representing a seedling sprouting from the earth, later associated with 'man' or 'male name'.
  - **interpretation:** Originally a pictogram representing soil and a growing plant, 甫 (fǔ, 'man') evolved to also symbolize a person, often used in names as a prefix denoting masculinity or adulthood.
- **examples:**
  - 他是一位正直的甫。
    - Tā shì yī wèi zhèngzhí de fǔ.
    - He is an upright man.
  - 古时(時)英豪皆尊甫为(為)表率。
    - Gǔshí yīngháo jiē zūn fǔ wéi biǎolǜ.
    - In ancient times, heroes all revered the man as a role model.
  - 文史名家赞扬这(讚揚這)位甫。
    - Wénshǐ míngjiā zànyáng zhè wèi fǔ.
    - Prominent writers and historians praised this man.
### 拍 → 尃 → 寸
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** cùn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - Line on the hand (ideographic) emphasizing the elbow ->
    - represents measurement unit between wrist and specific forearm position ->
    - meaning 'inch'
  - **interpretation:** 寸 (cùn, "inch") originated as a depiction of a line on the hand, indicating the area near the elbow. This specific placement was considered significant for pulse palpation, originally suggesting a forearm position, which then came to denote the measurement 'inch'.
- **examples:**
  - 这块(這塊)布每一寸都是精心制(製)作。
    - Zhè kuài bù měi yī cùn dōu shì jīngxīn zhìzuò.
    - Every inch of this cloth is crafted with care.
  - 请(請)用卷尺量一寸，每一寸数据(數據)都准确(準確)。
    - Qǐng yòng juǎnchǐ liàng yī cùn, měi yī cùn shùjù dōu zhǔnquè.
    - Please use a tape measure to measure an inch, every inch's data is accurate.
---
## 拍
### pāi

## to pat; to beat; to take (a picture)

## 秋天
---
## autumn
### qiūtiān
---
- **definition:** autumn
- **pinyin:** qiūtiān
- **components:**
  - 秋
    - qiū
    - autumn
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky; day; heavens
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:** 秋 (qiū, "autumn") and 天 (tiān, "sky; day; heavens") come together to refer to the season of autumn.
  - **interpretation:** The combination 秋 (qiū, "autumn") and 天 (tiān, "sky; day; heavens") denotes the time of year when autumn is present in the sky, symbolizing the autumn season. This aligns with the traditional division of the year into seasons observed in Chinese culture.
- **examples:**
  - 秋天来(來)了。
    - Qiūtiān láile.
    - Autumn has arrived.
  - 秋天的风(風)很凉(涼)爽，树叶开(樹葉開)始变黄(變黃)。
    - Qiūtiān de fēng hěn liángshuǎng, shùyè kāishǐ biàn huáng.
    - The autumn wind is cool, and the leaves begin to turn yellow.
  - 秋天到了，农(農)民开(開)始忙碌。
    - Qiūtiān dàole, nóngmín kāishǐ mánglù.
    - Autumn has come, and the farmers start to bustle about.
### 秋天 → 秋
- **definition:** autumn
- **pinyin:** qiū
- **components:**
  - 禾
    - hé
    - grain
  - 火
    - huǒ
    - fire
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - 禾 (hé, 'grain') + 火 (huǒ, 'fire') =
    - grain + fire ->
    - harvest time ->
    - autumn
  - **interpretation:** The character combines 'grain' and 'fire', symbolizing the practice of burning fields after harvest, marking autumn as harvest time.
- **examples:**
  - 秋天来(來)了。
    - Qiū tiān lái le.
    - Autumn has arrived.
  - 秋风(風)送爽，稻谷(穀)金黄(黃)。
    - Qiū fēng sòng shuǎng, dào gǔ jīn huáng.
    - The autumn breeze brings coolness, and the rice is golden.
  - 在秋季的午后，书(書)香满(滿)室。
    - Zài qiū jì de wǔ hòu, shū xiāng mǎn shì.
    - On an autumn afternoon, the room is filled with the fragrance of books.
### 秋天 → 秋 → 禾
- **definition:** grain
- **pinyin:** hé
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a stalk of grain or cereal plant
  - **interpretation:** The character 禾 (hé, 'grain') visually represents a plant with roots and leaves, focusing on the appearance of staple crops like rice or millet. This clearly conveys its meaning as it resembles the actual shape of a plant grown for its grain.
- **examples:**
  - 收获(穫)的禾香弥(彌)漫在田野中。
    - Shōuhuò de hé xiāng mímàn zài tiányě zhōng.
    - The fragrance of grain filled the fields.
  - 农(農)民辛勤耕作，收割禾穗。
    - Nóngmín xīnqín gēngzuò, shōugē hé suì.
    - The hardworking farmers harvested the ears of grain.
  - 春雨滋润(潤)了禾苗，预(預)示着丰(著豐)收。
    - Chūnyǔ zīrùn le hé miáo, yùshì zhe fēngshōu.
    - The spring rain nourished the grain seedlings, foreshadowing a bountiful harvest.
### 秋天 → 秋 → 火
- **definition:** fire
- **pinyin:** huǒ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts flames rising from a fire
  - **interpretation:** The character 火 (huǒ, "fire") visually represents flames flickering upwards, which intuitively conveys the essence of fire. This simple depiction is an effective way to capture the dynamic and essential nature of fire.
- **examples:**
  - 火在壁炉(爐)中熊熊燃烧(燒)。
    - Huǒ zài bìlú zhōng xióngxióng ránshāo.
    - The fire burns fiercely in the fireplace.
  - 野外露营时(營時)，火能驱(驅)走寒冷。
    - Yěwài lùyíng shí, huǒ néng qūzǒu hánlěng.
    - When camping outdoors, the fire can drive away the cold.
  - 遇到火灾时(災時)，迅速疏散最为(為)重要。
    - Yù dào huǒzāi shí, xùnsù shū sàn zuìwéi zhòngyào.
    - In case of a fire, evacuating quickly is of utmost importance.
### 秋天 → 天
- **definition:** sky; day; heavens
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜幕降临(臨)，天边(邊)星光闪烁(閃爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈求天佑众(眾)生。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.
---
## 秋天
### qiūtiān
---
## autumn
%%%
## 阴(陰)天( )
---
## cloudy sky; overcast weather
### yīntiān
---
- **traditional:** 陰天
- **definition:** cloudy sky; overcast weather
- **pinyin:** yīntiān
- **components:**
  - 阴(陰)
    - yīn
    - cloudy; overcast
  - 天
    - tiān
    - sky
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 陰(阴) (yīn, "cloudy; overcast") + 天 (tiān, "sky") =
    - "cloudy sky; overcast weather"
  - **interpretation:** A 天 (tiān, "sky") that is 陰(阴) (yīn, "cloudy") refers to weather conditions where the sky is covered with clouds, resulting in overcast weather. The combination succinctly conveys the concept of a day with gloomy weather.
- **examples:**
  - 今天是阴(陰)天，我们(們)打算待在家里(裡)。
    - Jīntiān shì yīntiān, wǒmen dǎsuàn dāi zài jiālǐ.
    - Today is overcast, and we plan to stay at home.
  - 阴(陰)天使得景色显(顯)得柔和。
    - Yīntiān shǐdé jǐngsè xiǎnde róuhé.
    - The cloudy sky makes the scenery appear soft.
  - 虽(雖)然今天是阴(陰)天，但心情却(卻)很晴朗。
    - Suīrán jīntiān shì yīntiān, dàn xīnqíng què hěn qínglǎng.
    - Although today is overcast, the mood is still quite bright.
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰)
- **traditional:** 陰
- **definition:** cloudy; overcast
- **pinyin:** yīn
- **components:**
  - 阜
    - fù
    - mound
  - 侌
    - yīn
    - phonetic
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Semantic: 阜 (fù, "mound") + Phonetic: 侌 (yīn) =
    - concealed places or shade ->
    - moon and female associations
  - **interpretation:** The character 阴(陰) (yīn, "concealed") uses 阜 (fù, "mound") to suggest a connection to physical features like hills or mounds that create shade, while 侌 (yīn) contributes the sound. This relates to concepts of concealment, shadow, and indirectly the moon and femininity in traditional Chinese thought.
  - **simplification:** The character 阴 replaces the phonetic 侌 (yīn) with 月 (yuè, "moon"), making it visually more simple and retaining the association with moon-related meanings.
- **examples:**
  - 北方的阴(陰)雨绵绵(綿綿)，让(讓)人感到忧郁(憂鬱)。
    - Běifāng de yīnyǔ miánmián, ràng rén gǎndào yōuyù.
    - The continuous gloomy drizzle in the north makes people feel depressed.
  - 她展现(現)出阴(陰)柔之美，令人着(著)迷。
    - Tā zhǎnxiàn chū yīnróu zhī měi, lìng rén zháomí.
    - She displays a unique feminine grace that captivates people.
  - 夜幕降临时(臨時)，月色显(顯)得格外阴(陰)柔。
    - Yèmù jiànglín shí, yuèsè xiǎndé géwài yīnróu.
    - As night falls, the moonlight appears especially soft and feminine.
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰) → 阜
- **definition:** mound
- **pinyin:** fù
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a mound or hill, with a shape that suggests an elevated landform.
  - **interpretation:** The character 阜 (fù, "mound") originally depicted the silhouette of a small hill or mound, representing its natural shape and structure.
- **examples:**
  - 山边(邊)的小阜上，盛开着(開著)野花。
    - Shān biān de xiǎo fù shàng, shèng kāi zhe yě huā.
    - Wildflowers bloom atop the small mound by the mountainside.
  - 古道尽头(盡頭)有阜。
    - Gǔ dào jìn tóu yǒu fù.
    - There is a mound at the end of the ancient road.
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 阴(陰) → 侌
- **definition:** phonetic
- **pinyin:** yīn
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ancient form
  - **description:** 侌 (yīn, "phonetic") → ancient form of 陰 (yīn, "yin; shade")
  - **interpretation:** The character 侌 originally served as a phonetic component in the composition of 陰 (yīn, "yin; shade"), suggesting its antique usage and historical derivation.
### 阴(陰)天( ) → 天
- **definition:** sky
- **pinyin:** tiān
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Horizontal line above 大(dà, "big") to depict sky ->
    - anthropomorphic man with large head symbolizing heaven
  - **interpretation:** The character 天(tiān) originally depicts the sky as a horizontal line above a person with outstretched arms, 大(dà, "big"), emphasizing the vastness or domain of heaven. Over time, the character evolved into an anthropomorphic representation of heaven, which later influenced its interpretation in classical texts.
- **examples:**
  - 夜幕降临(臨)，天边(邊)星光闪烁(閃爍)。
    - Yèmù jiànglín, tiānbiān xīnguāng shǎnshuò.
    - As night falls, starlight gleams on the horizon.
  - 他仰望高空，祈求天佑众(眾)生。
    - Tā yǎngwàng gāokōng, qíqiú tiānyòu zhòngshēng.
    - He gazes up to the sky and prays for heaven's protection over all living beings.

## 阴(陰)天( )
### yīntiān

## cloudy sky; overcast weather

## 下雪
---
## to snow
### xià xuě
---
- **definition:** to snow
- **pinyin:** xià xuě
- **components:**
  - 下
    - xià
    - fall; descend; under; next
  - 雪
    - xuě
    - snow; wipe away
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** compound word
  - **description:**
    - 下 (xià, "fall") + 雪 (xuě, "snow") =
    - when snow falls
  - **interpretation:** The term 下雪 (xià xuě) literally means 'snow fall' and is used to describe the meteorological event when snow descends from the sky.
- **examples:**
  - 昨晚下雪了。
    - Zuówǎn xià xuě le
    - It snowed last night.
  - 天越来(來)越冷，下雪的日子真美。
    - Tiān yuèláiyuè lěng, xià xuě de rìzi zhēn měi
    - The weather is getting colder, and snowy days are truly beautiful.
  - 一出门(門)就遇到下雪，心情就变(變)得愉快。
    - Yī chūmén jiù yùdào xià xuě, xīnqíng jiù biàn dé yúkuài
    - When I stepped out, it started snowing, and my mood instantly became cheerful.
### 下雪 → 下
- **definition:** fall; descend; under; next
- **pinyin:** xià
- **components:**
  - 一
    - yī
    - one
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:**
    - 一 (yī, "one") below horizontal line =
    - below ->
    - down
  - **interpretation:** The character 下(xià, "down") visually represents something placed below another object. The simple representation of a line under a horizontal stroke symbolically conveys the concept of 'down' or 'below'.
- **examples:**
  - 请(請)你下来(來)。
    - Qǐng nǐ xiàlái.
    - Please come down.
  - 他走下楼(樓)梯，进(進)入房间(間)。
    - Tā zǒu xià lóutī, jìnrù fángjiān.
    - He walked down the stairs and entered the room.
  - 雨下得很大，街道上满(滿)是积(積)水。
    - Yǔ xià de hěn dà, jiēdào shàng mǎn shì jīshuǐ.
    - It rained heavily, and the streets were full of puddles.
### 下雪 → 下 → 一
- **definition:** one
- **pinyin:** yī
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogram
  - **description:** A horizontal stroke representing the concept of 'one'.
  - **interpretation:** The character 一(yī, "one") is a simple horizontal line signifying the singular and unified concept of 'one'. It directly represents being singular or the number one.
- **examples:**
  - 我有一个苹(個蘋)果。
    - Wǒ yǒu yī gè píngguǒ.
    - I have one apple.
  - 他只看到一只鸟(隻鳥)，飞进(飛進)了花园(園)。
    - Tā zhǐ kàn dào yī zhī niǎo, fēi jìn le huā yuán.
    - He only saw one bird, which flew into the garden.
  - 一条(條)直路通向远(遠)方。
    - Yī tiáo zhí lù tōng xiàng yuǎn fāng.
    - One straight road leads to the distance.
### 下雪 → 雪
- **definition:** snow; wipe away
- **pinyin:** xuě
- **components:**
  - 雨
    - yǔ
    - rain
  - 彗
    - huì
    - broom
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Rain 雨 (yǔ, "rain") + Phonetic 彗 (huì, "broom") =
    - sweeping away rain ->
    - snow
  - **interpretation:** The combination of 雨 (yǔ, "rain") and 彗 (huì, "broom") effectively conveys the idea of snow as light, fluffy precipitation that resembles rain being swept away like with a broom, likely reflecting how snow covers surfaces.
  - **simplification:** The character 雪 is an ancient simplification of 䨮, both sharing the same components for rain and broom.
- **examples:**
  - 冬天来(來)了，雪花纷飞(紛飛)。
    - Dōngtiān láile, xuěhuā fēnfēi.
    - Winter has arrived, and snowflakes are fluttering.
  - 屋顶(頂)上挂着(掛著)雪。
    - Wūdǐng shàng guàzhe xuě.
    - Snow is hanging on the roof.
  - 初雪降临时(臨時)，万(萬)物银装(銀裝)。
    - Chū xuě jiànglín shí, wànwù yínzhuāng.
    - When the first snow arrives, everything is dressed in silver.
### 下雪 → 雪 → 雨
- **definition:** rain
- **pinyin:** yǔ
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:**
    - Depicts a cloud with drops of rain falling from it ->
    - horizontal stroke added later ->
    - rain
  - **interpretation:** 雨 (yǔ, "rain") visually represents rain falling from a cloud, capturing its essential form.
- **examples:**
  - 今天雨下得很大。
    - Jīntiān yǔ xià de hěn dà.
    - It rained hard today.
  - 他忘记带伞(記帶傘)，雨却(卻)毫不留情。
    - Tā wàngjì dài sǎn, yǔ què háobù liúqíng.
    - He forgot to bring an umbrella, and the rain showed no mercy.
  - 细(細)雨如丝(絲)，轻(輕)拂着(著)花瓣。
    - Xì yǔ rú sī, qīng fú zhe huā bàn.
    - The fine rain falls like silk, gently brushing the petals.
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗
- **definition:** broom
- **pinyin:** huì
- **components:**
  - 甡
    - shēn
    - broom
  - 又
    - yòu
    - hand
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 甡 (shēn, "broom") + 又 (yòu, "hand") =
    - holding a broom
  - **interpretation:** The character 彗 (huì, "broom") combines 甡 (shēn, "broom") with 又 (yòu, "hand") to depict the action of holding a broom. This emphasizes the function and use of a broom, suggesting an object specifically designed to be held by hand for sweeping.
- **examples:**
  - 他拿着(著)破旧(舊)的彗，清扫(掃)庭院。
    - Tā ná zhe pò jiù de huì, qīng sǎo tíng yuàn.
    - He holds the old broom and sweeps the courtyard.
  - 老匠人用彗，细致(細緻)打扫(掃)作坊。
    - Lǎo jiàngrén yòng huì, xìzhì dǎsǎo zuòfāng.
    - The old craftsman uses the broom to meticulously clean the workshop.
  - 在寒冬夜晚，他默默拿起彗，清扫门(掃門)前。
    - Zài hán dōng yè wǎn, tā mò mò ná qǐ huì, qīng sǎo mén qián.
    - On a cold winter night, he silently picked up the broom and swept the front door.
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡
- **definition:** broom
- **pinyin:** shēn
- **components:**
  - 生
    - shēng
    - birth
  - 辰
    - chén
    - time
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** phono-semantic compound
  - **description:**
    - Semantic: 生 (shēng, 'birth') + Phonetic: 辰 (chén, 'time') =
    - phonetic connection to 'shen' ->
    - interpretation related to extension or fullness
  - **interpretation:** The character 甡 combines 生 (shēng, 'birth'), suggesting growth or extension, with 辰 (chén, 'time'), providing the phonetic component. This blend implies a process of increase or expansion, which relates metaphorically to the meaning of a 'broom,' as it is an object that extends and clears space.
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 生
- **definition:** birth
- **pinyin:** shēng
- **components:**
  - 屮
    - chè
    - sprout
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** ideogrammic compound
  - **description:**
    - 屮 (chè, "sprout") on top of a horizontal line ->
    - signifies a plant sprouting from the ground ->
    - symbolizes life
  - **interpretation:** The character 生 (shēng, "life") represents the concept of life force or vitality, symbolized by a sprout emerging from the earth, embodying growth and renewal.
- **examples:**
  - 生命是一场(場)美丽(麗)的旅程。
    - Shēngmìng shì yī chǎng měilì de lǚchéng.
    - Life is a beautiful journey.
  - 他在战场(戰場)上奋(奮)力生存。
    - Tā zài zhànchǎng shàng fènlì shēngcún.
    - He fights to live on the battlefield.
  - 这(這)家餐厅(廳)的生鱼(魚)片非常新鲜(鮮)。
    - Zhè jiā cāntīng de shēngyúpiàn fēicháng xīnxiān.
    - The raw fish slices at this restaurant are very fresh.
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 生 → 屮
- **definition:** sprout
- **pinyin:** chè
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a sprout emerging from the ground
  - **interpretation:** 屮 (chè, 'sprout') is a pictogram that directly represents a young plant or sprout emerging from the ground. Its visual form captures the essence of new growth, and it historically served as an early representation of plant life or new vegetation.
- **examples:**
  - 春雨滋润后(潤後)，小屮冲(沖)破泥土而出。
    - chūn yǔ zī rùn hòu, xiǎo chè chōng pò ní tǔ ér chū.
    - After the spring rain nurtured the earth, the little sprout broke through the soil.
  - 草屮初生露尖端。
    - cǎo chè chū shēng lù jiān duān.
    - The grass sprout's tip has just emerged.
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 甡 → 辰
- **definition:** time
- **pinyin:** chén
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a heavenly body or a celestial presence, often associated with dragons in ancient mythology.
  - **interpretation:** 辰 (chén, "early form of dragon") originally depicted a celestial body that was believed to influence time and was associated with dragons due to mythological links between dragons and celestial phenomena.
- **examples:**
  - 古代传说(傳說)中的辰是神秘而强(強)大的生物。
    - Gǔdài chuánshuō zhōng de chén shì shénmì ér qiángdà de shēngwù.
    - In ancient legends, the chén is a mysterious and powerful creature.
  - 东(東)方初升的朝阳(陽)映照着(著)辰的鳞(鱗)光，唤(喚)起了古老的神话(話)。
    - Dōngfāng chūshēng de cháoyáng yìngzhào zhe chén de línguāng, huànqǐ le gǔlǎo de shénhuà.
    - The rising morning sun in the east illuminates the scales of the chén, evoking ancient myths.
  - 传(傳)承了古老智慧的文献记载(獻記載)了辰的奇迹(蹟)，使后(後)人对(對)它充满(滿)敬畏。
    - Chuánchéng le gǔlǎo zhìhuì de wénxiàn jìzǎi le chén de qíjī, shǐ hòurén duì tā chōngmǎn jìngwèi.
    - Ancient texts carrying old wisdom recorded the miracles of the chén, filling later generations with awe.
### 下雪 → 雪 → 彗 → 又
- **definition:** hand
- **pinyin:** yòu
- **etymology:**
  - **type:** pictogram
  - **description:** Depicts a right hand
  - **interpretation:** The character 又 (yòu, "hand") is a pictogram representing a right hand, showing the fingers and palm, which highlights its original meaning related to manual actions.
- **examples:**
  - 「又」这个字最早来源于手(「又」這個字最早來源於手)。
    - 「Yòu」 zhè gè zì zuì zǎo láiyuán yú shǒu。
    - The character '又' originally comes from the hand.
  - 很多汉(漢)字含有又部首，表示与(與)手有关(關)的动(動)作。
    - Hěn duō hànzì hányǒu Yòu bùshǒu, biǎoshì yǔ shǒu yǒuguān de dòngzuò。
    - Many Chinese characters include the '又' radical, indicating actions related to the hand.
  - 古人用又描绘(繪)手的形态(態)，体现(體現)了古汉(漢)字的独(獨)特魅力。
    - Gǔrén yòng Yòu miáohuì shǒu de xíngtài, tǐxiàn le gǔ hànzì de dútè mèilì。
    - Ancient people used '又' to depict the shape of the hand, showcasing the unique charm of ancient Chinese characters.
